# License Overview | EnGenius Cloud Licensing

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/#start-with-essential-features-and-upgrade-with-pro-licenses)

**Start with essential features and upgrade with Pro licenses.**

EnGenius Cloud provides two types of feature plans, _**Basic and PRO**_. You need to set up the feature plan to either Basic or PRO for product categories.

The _**Basic**_ feature plan comes with essential cloud features for free, and the _**PRO**_ plan requires a Pro license to enable managed devices with professional features.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3299519939-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MkFTP6mPDb3kJRwf2Rb%252Fuploads%252Fkv3VNRZowpCiphKjAmF3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D325525a0-998a-4752-bbff-71357e3a91ad&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=38302578&sv=2)

Diagram 1 - Feature Plan for

*   Users can choose any feature plan combination for different device categories. For example, you only need basic management features of Switches but require professional features of Access Points.
    
*   Each device category will follow its Feature Plan(_**Basic**_ _or_ _**PRO**_) to keep the logs and capacity of advanced features accordingly.
    
*   System-wide features like “admin users count, and Network limitation…etc.” will remain PRO as long as there is one _**PRO**_ feature plan is enabled for any device category.
    
*   Users can change the feature plan between _**Basic**_ _and_ _**PRO**_ anytime.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3299519939-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MkFTP6mPDb3kJRwf2Rb%252Fuploads%252FFShFPXm4FcOXzOYa5N03%252Fnew%2520license%2520page.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D08550d3e-9667-4dde-bb23-c439b7bbbf75&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d61a04f&sv=2)

When a device category is switched from _**PRO**_ _to_ _**Basic**_, all privileges that exceed the limit of the _**Basic**_ plan will be erased and all professional features related will be disabled.

**Feature Plan Comparison:**

Click here to see the full comparison table. (Basic vs. PRO)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/#engenius-cloud-is-per-device-licensing)

**EnGenius Cloud is per-device licensing**

The **EnGenius Cloud License** on each device operates independently. Per-device licensing allows the IT managers to manage the validity of single or multiple licenses across sites and regions. In addition, per-device licensing makes network management more effortless.

Users with _**Org admin privilege**_ can associate the license to any registered device. Once you assign this _**license-associated device**_ to any Network in your Organization, the license is activated and will expire after the license term defined in the license model, as measured from the activation date.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/#simple-and-straightforward-management-of-per-device-licensing)

Simple and straightforward management of Per-device licensing

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3299519939-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MkFTP6mPDb3kJRwf2Rb%252Fuploads%252F8QyKPVdAswdNsbrmbgdS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De318d7da-6978-452e-9959-c7afcdae9d49&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61eb644c&sv=2)

Diagram 2 - Per-device licensing

*   Each license can only be associated with one device _(Device A)_
    
*   A Device can have multiple licenses associated with it to extend the expired date _(Device B)_
    
*   Devices might have different license expired dates based on the valid duration you associated with it. _(Device A, B)_
    
*   All devices of the same category within the **Organization** must follow the same Feature Plan _(Basic/ PRO)_
    

Last updated 12 days ago

# Signing Up | Cloud User Manual

Before you start to manage EnGenius devices, you must first sign up for the service.

Registering EnGenius Cloud is similar to other web-based platforms and can be done either with a social media account (e.g., Google or Facebook) or by creating an account from scratch. You will need to provide your email address, company name, physical address, and phone number. Furthermore, you must determine the country in which your account will be hosted. That is, all relative device information, user configurations, and client statistics will be kept in the corresponding region of servers (**Oregon** for the US, **Irland** for the EU, **Tokyo** for JP, **Mumbai** for APAC except Japan). This enables EnGenius Cloud to protect customer data and comply with requirements like **GDPR** for customers within the European Union.

Support for signing up with EnGenius Partner Portal is already available.

Last updated 1 month ago

Was this helpful?

# Troubleshooting ECW AP | Cloud User Manual

1.  Check the [LED Status](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup/troubleshooting-ecw-ap/led-status)
     to see if any problem encountered. If Power LED keeps flashing for over 10 minutes, then there could be Cloud connection issues.
    
2.  Use your mobile phone to scan if Default SSID of the AP found. (you have to be around the AP location) From the Default SSID, you can also identify which stage the AP is stuck on. See [details of Default SSID](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup/troubleshooting-ecw-ap/default-ssids)
    .
    
3.  To troubleshoot the connection issue, you may login to Local page:
    
    1.  Use your client device (e.g., a laptop, mobile device, or tablet) to ﬁnd the SSID: “EnMGMTxxxx” (xxxx is the last four digits of LAN MAC which can be found on the back of the device) and connect to it.
        
    2.  Enter the URL in web browser: [http://EnGenius.local](http://engenius.local/)
         or the IP 192.168.1.1 to access the device’s user interface. You can review device status after logging into the AP with the default account/password ( default admin account/ password : admin/ admin.)
        
    

_**Issue: Cannot find Default SSID**_

1\. Check for available wireless networks (Check if a known [default SSID](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup/troubleshooting-ecw-ap/default-ssids)
 is being broadcast).

2\. If a default SSID is being broadcast, connect your device to it.

3\. If no known default SSIDs are present, set up a manual wireless network connection. For the SSID name, use 'EnMGMT', e.g. 'EnMGMTxxxx', where the x's are replaced with the last four digits of the LAN MAC address.

4\. After connecting, open a web browser and connect to one of the local access page addresses.

Last updated 1 year ago

# Getting Started | Cloud User Manual

This session will assist you in setting up a new network on the EnGenius Cloud web application. For easier, faster setup, use the EnGenius Cloud for iOS or EnGenius Cloud for Android mobile apps. No matter which version you start with, you can always switch seamlessly between the web and mobile.

This article is not meant to be a comprehensive list of everything EnGenius Cloud, but rather a stepping stone to get started in the most informed way possible.

Last updated 5 years ago

# Device Setup | Cloud User Manual

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup#ecw-ap-installation)

**ECW AP Installation**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup#ecw-ap-package-contents)

**ECW AP Package Contents**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LnvdfwHTAg_75b6M18W%252F-LnvivU6GT2px7HIZCSX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7b134ba-32cd-4d5e-b541-5c7a58aa33ff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9401dd85&sv=2)

ECW220/230 Package Contents

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup#ecw115)

\-ECW115

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-M8V-nJtmxy1-29npJfh%252F-M8V0jt6PlUdHfao0TLm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd50d9a94-aaac-43ff-b102-a069d958f27c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2bebc2c6&sv=2)

ECW115 Package Contents

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup#minimum-access-requirement)

**Minimum Access Requirement**

**Power source option** - An ECW AP device can be powered by an 802.3af/at-compliant PoE device or by DC12V input

Do not use both power sources at the same time.

**Ethernet port:**

*   LAN (PoE): Uplink port accepts an 802.3af/at power source.
    
*   LAN2: Data link if this port is built on a device.
    

**Connect the AP to Internet:**

You need to find a way to let the Cloud AP be able to access internet, so it can be managed by EnGenius Cloud.

*   **Connect the uplink LAN port to a switch port or port of router**: This is the most common way to let AP be able to access Internet. (Note: please make sure the port is internet accessible by connecting a notebook to the port and browse the internet)
    
*   **Use your existing Cloud-managed ECW AP to mesh the new AP**: Sometimes the place the AP installed is not accessible with Ethernet cable, then you can leverage EnGenius Mesh technology to mesh the new AP to your existing cloud-managed ECW AP.
    
*   After internet connected, you will see Power LED blinking until the AP is able to communicate with EnGenius Cloud and the LED becomes steady lid. Usually it will take about 8 mins if there is new firmware available to upgrade.
    
*   If the LED keeps blinking, then there could be some issues like no IP address, or local proxy server setting required...etc. To set static IP or Proxy, or managed VLAN, you can login to Local Access Page through Managed SSID of the AP.
    

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup#ecs-switch-installation)

**ECS Switch Installation**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup#ecs-switch-package-contents)

**ECS Switch Package Contents**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lo4dNAMCEWp5y6s2FjY%252F-Lo4depWZoP7DI3t8xJU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7bdc7d67-7e40-4845-8a77-547ba5bff556&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3fff212&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup#connecting-to-ecs-switch)

**Connecting to ECS Switch**

**A)** Connect the supplied power adapter (or power cord) to the switch and plug the other end into an electrical outlet. Verify the power LED indicator is lit on the switch. Wait for the switch to complete boot up. It might take few minutes to complete the process.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lo4dNAMCEWp5y6s2FjY%252F-Lo4g2EjvevpcJF7fnTT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D468e50ff-8d3f-421f-9963-310008de009c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c8173336&sv=2)

**B)** Connect one end of a category 5/6 Ethernet cable into the gigabit (10/100/1000) Ethernet port on the switch’s front panel and the other end to the Ethernet port on the computer. Verify that the LED on the Ethernet port of the switch is green.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lo4dNAMCEWp5y6s2FjY%252F-Lo4gPWyAhNkjcMKekWU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05dac46b-3fe5-4b19-aa71-f346fd3642aa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2af7dc51&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup#login-to-the-ecs-switch-local-access-page)

**Login to the ECS Switch Local Access Page**

The switch's default IP address setting is DHCP client mode, which will get an IP address from the DHCP server. It will automatically change to static IP address assignment if the switch cannot get an IP address from the DHCP server within two minutes of booting up.

If your switch cannot get an IP address from local DHCP server, or you would like to use static IP address assignment, you may follow the below procedures to manage your computer connection to the switch via a static IP address.

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup#ip-address-configuration-on-your-computer)

**IP address configuration on your computer:**

A) Once your computer is on, configure the settings of your network adapter. Open Network Connections > Local Area Connection > Internet Protocol Version 4 (TCP/IPv4) > Properties

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lo4dNAMCEWp5y6s2FjY%252F-Lo4k088COFDdhoIl9jZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D328bef5f-f78f-4fc7-9b90-6f1b441b405b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fcab3278&sv=2)

B) Select **Use the following IP address** and make the following entries:

*   **IP Address:** 192.168.0.10 (or any address in the 192.168.0.x network)
    
*   **Subnet mask:** 255.255.255.0
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lo4dNAMCEWp5y6s2FjY%252F-Lo4mfe9IymP3rALZyZD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcdaba94e-069e-45f7-b44c-4fb65d4d70c7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81b42f78&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup#login-to-ecs-switch)

**Login to ECS Switch**

**A)** Open a web browser on your computer. In the address bar of the web browser, enter the ECS switch IP address and hit enter.

**B)** The default username is **admin** and the password is **password**. **We strongly recommend that you change these as soon as possible.** Enter the username and password of the switch and then click Login.

\*Your model number may be different in the web browser interface.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lo4dNAMCEWp5y6s2FjY%252F-Lo4p7YkQ2l0KixTeagj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22fb97b2-5a62-4700-a790-dbb623552163&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=993a45e3&sv=2)

**C)** ECS Switch local access page will appear.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lo4rMDah48vzHzyvrhY%252F-Lo4reHFwW3GpTT_JUb0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D62dfcf32-0e44-4a26-b426-dba78fbc805f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5eea046b&sv=2)

Instead of default DHCP settings on ECS switch, users may choose a static IP address setting for their deployed network. Remember to open **System** > **Static Route** to setup the static IP address/gateway settings on the switch in this case.

Last updated 5 years ago

# Registering Devices to Organization | Cloud User Manual

Before devices can be assigned to the network, they must be registered to an Organization that you preferred in advance.

1.  Locate the serial number located on the bottom of the device.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FXqxq7BXpeplQ3kBhb5Xi%252F1660789075749.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47bc40ac-ea09-4809-8fb8-e0a6db284603&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81c366e5&sv=2)

2\. Navigate to **Organization** \> **Inventory & License** and click th**e Register Device** on the top of the table.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F7sjv7ebfSIvTN0vCDVq3%252F1660790666650.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D762eecfb-8425-4417-ae3a-77bffc4cc4bd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e0115fe3&sv=2)

3\. Enter the serial number that you located in the device and enter them. If you have multiple devices you can enter the SN one per row, so devices could be registered at once. And then click the **Register** button.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FH7V0BjIDBBx8JtEZZJBY%252F1660790775733.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db876b86c-207c-4033-9ed0-a17034ecd976&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=349827ad&sv=2)

# Logging On | Cloud User Manual

Once your account has been created, you can login to EnGenius Cloud in the following steps:

1.  Open a web browser to [https://cloud.engenius.ai/](https://cloud.engenius.ai/)
     . This will bring up the main login page.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lo3aQIhxLeS6TYgeDfZ%252F-Lo3aU5nOxp_COEZte2Y%252F1567738782404.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17503444-bcfd-4c04-9075-5245e60b1aa9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4b9276c5&sv=2)

2\. Enter your EnGenius Cloud email address and password and click the **Sign in** button.

3\. For EnGenius Partner who has account on EnGenius Partner Portal already, you can simply click on "E Partner" button, and EnGenius Partner Portal will pop up login page for you to use Single-Sign-On capability of Partner Portal to log on to EnGenius Cloud

4\. For Google and Facebook users, you can also click on "Google" or "Facebook" button to use your account on Google and Facebook to log on to EnGenius Cloud

5\. EnGenius Cloud will create a new default Organization and Network for every new account based on the email address as unique user identification. (note: If someone is invited to an Organization or Network, this account won't have default Organization and Network.) If you have multiple accounts created on EnGenius Cloud, EnGenius Cloud will merge your accounts based on the "email address" of the account. For example, if you have created a new account on EnGenius Cloud using the same email address as your google account, then you're able to login to this email account either through Google account authentication with Google account password, or through EnGenius Cloud Login with the password while you created the EnGenius Cloud account.

Last updated 1 month ago

Was this helpful?

# Assigning Devices to Network | Cloud User Manual

# What is EnGenius Cloud? | Cloud User Manual

Other Languages: [日本語](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-jp/)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud#before-you-begin)

Before You Begin

To start using the EnGenius Cloud service, you must prepare the following:

*   At least one supported EnGenius Cloud wireless access point or switch.
    
*   An existing network with an Internet connection including DHCP and DNS configuration.
    

You can also install the "EnGenius Cloud" mobile app (available for both iOS and Android) for easier device registration and monitoring.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud#supported-web-browsers)

Supported Web Browsers

The EnGenius Cloud is primarily accessible with a web browser. Before signing up for the EnGenius Cloud service or logging on to the web interface to manage your network, first verify that you are using a supported browser.

The following table lists the web browsers that EnGenius Cloud supports:

Browser

Release

Google Chrome

57.0.2987.110 and later

Mozilla Firefox

52.0 and later

Microsoft Edge

80.0.361.103 and later

If you use an unsupported web browser, you may experience issues displaying elements on the web interface.

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

# Login to Local Access Page | Cloud User Manual

1.  Use your client device (e.g., a laptop, mobile device, or tablet) to find the SSID: “EnMGMTxxxx” (xxxx is the last four digits of the MAC address, found on the back of the device) and connect to it.
    
2.  Under your web browser, enter the URL [http://EnGenius.local](http://engenius.local/)
     or the localhost IP address (192.168.1.1) to access the device’s user interface. You can review device status after logging into the AP with the default admin account/password (default account & password: **admin**/**admin**)
    

By default, EnGenius cloud access points (ECW series) are assigned an IP address dynamically by the DHCP server. If you encounter issues with IP address assignment, please double check that the IP settings include IP address, subnet mask, gateway, proxy, and management VLAN. If any issues still exist, you may change your IP assignment from "DHCP mode" to "Static IP" via the following procedure:

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LnvdfwHTAg_75b6M18W%252F-LnvnHGt38SjJX1zzXOq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D18be00fb-0eb6-4627-a44d-76f3653b6e1e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7aa0379&sv=2)

ECW AP's Local Access Page

By default, EnGenius cloud access points (ECW series) are assigned an IP address dynamically by the DHCP server. If you encounter issues with IP address assignment, please double check that the IP settings including IP address, subnet mask, gateway, proxy, and management VLAN. If any issues still exist, you may change your IP assignment from "DHCP mode" to "Static IP" via the following procedure:

a) Select “Local Setting” on this page.

b) Change IPv4 setting from “AS DHCP client” to “Use Static IP”

c) Configure the IP address, gateway, net mask, and proxy policy as required.

d) Reconnect this device to the LAN again if necessary.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup/troubleshooting-ecw-ap/login-to-local-access-page#local-access-page-options)

**Local Access Page Options**

Every device's status page includes useful information about the status of the device, basic configuration options (such as setting a static IP), and other tools. The following section will explain the items available on the device status page.

ECW Access Points provide the following information and configuration options on their local status page:

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup/troubleshooting-ecw-ap/login-to-local-access-page#device-status-section)

**Device Status Section**

Contains information regarding the device overview, EnGenius Cloud overview, and network connectivity information.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lo4396cnzwD1zvMFbZx%252F-Lo48-PhpbTaf_1Yo-Ow%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50c22d8f-ae75-431c-96a7-5f39bfae4718&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90309a06&sv=2)

Device Status on Local Access Page

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup/troubleshooting-ecw-ap/login-to-local-access-page#device-overview)

**Device Overview**

Provides information regarding the name, model, serial number, IP address, MAC address, and current firmware.

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup/troubleshooting-ecw-ap/login-to-local-access-page#cloud-overview)

**Cloud Overview**

Provides information about the Cloud registration status, date of registration, and time of last update.

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup/troubleshooting-ecw-ap/login-to-local-access-page#network-connectivity)

**Network Connectivity**

Provides connectivity information to local network, Internet, and EnGenius Cloud.

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/getting-started/device-setup/troubleshooting-ecw-ap/login-to-local-access-page#local-setting-section)

**Local Setting Section**

Provides settings for IPv4 / IPv6 address, management VLAN, firmware upgrade, and other miscellaneous configuration items (such as HTTP/HTTPS Proxy). Users can also reboot the device or reset the device to factory default settings from here.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lo4396cnzwD1zvMFbZx%252F-Lo49CTS8XyrzLMSYjki%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59adb8c4-ce91-42c5-b66e-116796c6648e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=51f1877c&sv=2)

Local Setting on Local Access page

The HTTP proxy only allows all default management traffic from the EnGenius ECW device to be sent through a proxy.

# Organization | Cloud User Manual

A collection of hierarchy views and networks that are part of a single organizational entity, such as a company or school district. Each organization is the owner of a single license.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/working-with-org-trees/organizations#adding-an-organization)

Adding an organization


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click **Menu > Create Organization** button to create organization

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LkNDwf3gSsdfSVtoJFU%252F-LkNInuXiCsawmNMaew8%252F1563775847239.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71cd8960-5d21-41cb-ae58-34379910e5db&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=79058c37&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/working-with-org-trees/organizations#edit-organization)

Edit Organization


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Edit a organization if you need to update any its current settings (for example, if you want to change the Organization name, Country, TimeZone.)

Follow these steps to edit a Organization.

1.  Click **Menu > Find the Organization you want to edit > Edit**
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Ll9sgjozGySx97R_jlx%252F-Ll9t93cqEn3eKCUXeFn%252F1564624435642.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01587c09-26c1-4408-8c28-a155f110fee9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e4a18a8&sv=2)

2\. Update Network Settings as required

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LkXw2aGJyc2LbJTmYJN%252F-LkXwO-LhwQDk1bIzOhK%252Fezmcloud_-Add_New_Organization%25402x%255B1%255D.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d841459-eb16-4490-8327-c803d6ff3b3d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=340115df&sv=2)

3\. Click **Apply**

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/working-with-org-trees/organizations#delete-organization)

Delete **Organization**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you no longer need a Organization that you previously created, you can delete it.

Follow these steps to delete a organization

1.  Click **Menu > Find the Organization you want to edit > Delete**
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Llj6KT7w-a3F-7_E2iM%252F-Llj6Qi2cHqBrLlLBb0s%252F1565232138565.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e1b1290-2491-4de0-a0b9-240062ad91fc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=39935229&sv=2)

2\. Popup is displayed and click **Confirm**

# Working with Organization Trees | Cloud User Manual

EnGenius Cloud adopts an organization tree structure to let user define the scope of their managed networks. All device managing or monitoring functions can be applied to different scopes as laid out in the user's tree. That gives VAR or MSP users great flexibility in managing their networks.

The current organization tree structure consists of three levels, from largest to smallest:

*   Organization - A grouping of one or more hierarchies under the umbrella of a single license.
    
*   Hierarchy View - A cluster of networks, which may be geographically concentrated or spread out.
    
*   Network - A set of network devices united by a single configuration set.
    

The organization tree definition is shown on the top left corner of the web GUI as follows:

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LoO2Xrco5PcBfj2cVQ0%252F-LoO2ZzgDGv9G4EYe7PR%252F1568083393107.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab8989c5-7771-4b28-82da-3fc363d72ffc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c81de9df&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/working-with-org-trees#how-to-videos)

**How-to Videos**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/working-with-org-trees#how-to-build-your-company-networks-in-engenius-cloud)

**How to build your company networks in EnGenius Cloud**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LoO3pWrFLHTKkrlB7lY%252F-LoO5-NTbWnRpEj2Edkr%252F1568084031896.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc5f8c767-25ea-4975-aa2f-f95d802bb948&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a555f4b0&sv=2)

# Hierarchy View | Cloud User Manual

A hierarchy view is a group of networks and/or nested hierarchy views. It follows a tree-like structure much like folders on your computer's operating system.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/working-with-org-trees/hyperviews#adding-a-hierarchy-view)

Adding a hierarchy view


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can create hierarchy views for a new organization or an existing organization, or even within an existing hierarchy view. Click **Menu** > **Choose organization or hierarchy view > Add hierarchy view**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Ll5zsMCADFU6Tfe9OFT%252F-Ll5zuAVQmb4MPjTn5Sl%252F1564553004830.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1e1941bf-7580-4eb0-a417-d34b49158c15&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c4c469e6&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/working-with-org-trees/hyperviews#edit-hierarchy-views)

Edit hierarchy views


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  You can edit the name of a hierarchy view name by clicking **Menu** > **Choose hierarchy view** **\> Edit**
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LnFwqP3erR54DRi6EB9%252F-LnFxs-_OcieEETJteIK%252F1566873536341.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D584ebbf9-257a-4c02-818a-af462577810d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98707e01&sv=2)

2\. Change the **Hierarchy View** name and click **Apply.**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lo4HnOJWl2_eGZa4cSv%252F-Lo4Hq2l4WHHUZckbXxi%252F1567751869542.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44e2fbaa-0ddd-4b99-92de-57bb61cdc5d3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=edffbf5b&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/working-with-org-trees/hyperviews#delete-hierarchy-view)

Delete Hierarchy View


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can delete hierarchy views by clicking **Menu** > **Choose hierarchy view** and then clicking on the garbage icon.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lo4GKE2c5H3Ada5ASzq%252F-Lo4HLxwc6i1hJXjNPqo%252F1567751741741.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D524c55bf-2485-468f-a863-aef6e20c7e57&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bd61e4f6&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/working-with-org-trees/hyperviews#move-network-under-hierarchy-view)

Move Network under Hierarchy View


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After created Networks and associate devices, if the HV is changed, say, the Network originally belongs to North Region, and now become North-East Region, users have to change the HV and would like to move the Network under North-Region to North-East-Region. This allows users to "drag & drop" any Network to new HV under same Organization.

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

# Network | Cloud User Manual

A network contains a list of devices and relevant information, such as configuration, SSID, radio settings, and firmware upgrade history. Each network contains a single configuration set for its devices, so if you have multiple configurations for devices, you can create a separate network to handle that.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/working-with-org-trees/networks#adding-a-network)

Adding a network


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Click **Menu > Choose organization or hierarchy > Create network**
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LkYL4c4NDgi2Bh3esWp%252F-LkYL6spKcNo86GDfcB7%252F1563961068936.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd694e2fe-32db-4f59-a31d-da91604e8bf3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c4310dc2&sv=2)

2\. Enter a **name** for the network, select the **country**, **time zone,** and then click **Create.**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lo3fnabFG5RP-1TDWRY%252F-Lo3fp8dtNbx_RGpo7gn%252F1567741633873.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b27992c-7ecd-4f1c-8d9c-bf0c81c3b9ab&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d9fdf43&sv=2)

If total networks in an Organization are more than 500, Users might experience unexpected slow responses or issues on Cloud.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/working-with-org-trees/networks#edit-network)

Edit Network


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Network name**, **country**, and **timezone** can be edited as needed. Follow the steps below to edit a network.

**Choose network** **\> Edit**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LkYLc_MznOKf_3d5rFv%252F-LkYLh8hqjPuZiUCiTRo%252F1563961223000.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6dd498cc-1bfe-47f5-b4f2-a3117da7d431&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ecfed6d0&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/working-with-org-trees/networks#delete-network)

Delete Network


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you no longer need a network that you previously created, you can delete it.

Follow these steps to delete a network.

1.  Click **Menu > Choose network > Delete**
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LkYNzdaWwy1kRFbL8Jb%252F-LkYO6DFt9nchONvpVZi%252F1563961794738.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69ea1bb9-6368-4d17-a801-bf93a0c9d210&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f4ed607d&sv=2)

2\. Popup is displayed. Click **Confirm.**

# Managing Camera | Cloud User Manual

There are two ways for users to quickly pick up cameras for deeper inspection. Camera List can handle regular maintenance with plenty of information, while Camera Grid is the perfect way for video event investigation. Users can switch between the two modes for all cameras. Cameras can be shown here after being registered to the cloud and assigned to a network. To manage the cameras in a network, trigger the toolbar menu on the left-hand side: **Manage > Cameras**.

Last updated 3 months ago

ECW AP's


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The first step is to get the serial numbers of the Cloud equipment you want to add to your cloud account. The serial number can be found on the box of the Cloud AP (ECW) or Cloud switch (ECS). An example of each is below:

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-M8F73usFyHvmInKQ0wi%252F-M8FAB-vSM9OO9C6Y4qT%252F1590482987625.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D98568c81-57f4-4f60-b948-00e919fce2ec&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ce21632c&sv=2)

Fig 1: ECW Serial number on box

1.  Model number of ECW AP
    

2\. Serial Number of ECW AP (This string of information that is added in the Cloud GUI)

3\. Hardware version on ECW AP

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-M8F73usFyHvmInKQ0wi%252F-M8FBOtxxvYJrXo64GQ0%252F1590483211038.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc697dd0c-d11c-4720-9427-7be1be6610ce&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2cafba81&sv=2)

# Region & Cross Lines | Cloud User Manual

Regions and lines are a useful tool to identify specific areas of interest in your camera’s field of view. These both can be configured in the **Monitor** > **Camera > Detail > Region & Line**

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details/region-and-cross-lines#drawing-a-region-for-region-counting)

Drawing a Region for Region Counting


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details/region-and-cross-lines#steps)

Steps

1.  Mouse to click and draw a polygon by placing points on the camera’s screenshot.
    
2.  Click each point sequentially to form the region.
    
3.  Complete the region by connecting the last point back to the first point
    
4.  You can adjust each point. If finished click apply.
    

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details/region-and-cross-lines#drawing-a-line-for-crossing-line-counting)

Drawing a Line for Crossing Line Counting


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details/region-and-cross-lines#steps-1)

Steps

1.  Click on the starting point of the line within the camera's field of view.
    
2.  Drag the line to the endpoint and click to place it. you can click the arrow icon to change the in/out direction.
    
3.  Adjust the point location after you com
    
4.  Click Apply
    

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details/region-and-cross-lines#undefined)


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details/region-and-cross-lines#region-activity)

Region Activity


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This will show on **camera detail > Summary**. Users can switch between “All Regions” and each region available. The numbers displayed on the charts represent the total people within the drawn region.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252Fq1asFesHpzdW5Hvuy0FV%252F1734511229202.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6cbeebf7-9d2d-474b-a82d-9846b92d8dba&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17204d9d&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details/region-and-cross-lines#line-activity)

Line Activity


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This will show on **camera detail > summary**. The user can switch between “All Lines” and each line available. The numbers displayed on the charts represent the total people In/Out traffic cross the drawn line.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FEzuNj3AsAkj1dnLTfCPR%252F1734512995606.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6b620723-ef2e-4fb7-a9f7-5b710b98fcae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4666ffd2&sv=2)

# Recording Playback and smart Motion Search | Cloud User Manual

Live view, playback, and smart motion search are combined into one panel to reduce switching operations between each other. Normally, users spend time searching for videos on the timeline. Here smart Motion search makes it easy and reduces the number of times to play back and forward on record track

you can access Video Playback from **Monitor > Camera > Videos**

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/recording-playback-and-smart-motion-search#timeline-search)

Timeline Search


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FjMTSRQ3qLUfR2AAVVXgg%252F1735541358651.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da7880dcd-f9c1-4911-99a7-422f5dc8863a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=92786091&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/recording-playback-and-smart-motion-search#steps)

Steps

1.  Pick a specific day and time on the calendar.
    
2.  Scroll on record track and then mouse up and down to the appropriate duration scale where event stamps on the timeline are clear.
    
3.  Click pre- or next-events on the timeline, or mouse over the timeline to pop up an event snapshot and click on the timestamp to the time point.
    
4.  Once abnormality is found, click pre- or next frame to locate a clear moment and take a snapshot or export a video clip.
    

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/recording-playback-and-smart-motion-search#smart-motion-search)

Smart Motion Search


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This allows you to identify people and vehicles within the camera's field of view and quickly find relevant events.

You can click the **smart motion search** on the top-right corner at the beginning.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FFfx1bmi1jKS4HQoKAttC%252F1735542366767.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D096099ac-8805-4ea3-8f5f-b3a94c0b91de&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d152102e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/recording-playback-and-smart-motion-search#steps-1)

Steps

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FYg2VnFNuCeDuu6fdI6Za%252F1735543151385.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0dceac5-c52d-43ff-be1d-d6c18c217e7a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=143e8d2f&sv=2)

1.  Set an interest region on video. Results are shown on paging, sorting from latest to past.
    
2.  Check the snapshot or scroll down to the next page of results. Once an abnormality was found, click on the snapshot to playback the video clip on the timeline. Each time duration can have multiple search result , you can click right or left arrow icon to find it.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FILvHUKXtEsezN02600re%252F1736746967869.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D313899bb-b588-42ab-8d68-a91109b16b92&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e42201e&sv=2)

1.  Once you can't find the results you want, you can click the filter icon to search based on the time duration.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F0bACrskThsatEPombw7s%252F1736745597188.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D62181a5e-7f54-40c9-b8da-2cdd74382bc5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6df18f96&sv=2)

1.  Click pre- or next frame to locate a clear moment and take a snapshot or export a video clip.
    

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/recording-playback-and-smart-motion-search#people-search)

People Search


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This allows you to identify people within the camera's field of view and quickly find relevant events.

The details steps are the same when you do the motion search, but change to the People tab.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FUlEJRegv3sKiPJz42Fav%252F1735543400667.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28a9a96b-db52-48d0-8bd8-32ee3a361ccb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0d1f8c0&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/recording-playback-and-smart-motion-search#vehicle-search)

Vehicle Search


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This allows you to identify vehicles within the camera's field of view and quickly find relevant events.

The details steps are the same when you do the motion search, but change to the Vehicle tab.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FLI4oWy9LSm9AMoWFLSZQ%252F1735543413468.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7529b59f-78b7-4fe9-a06e-75ec0b576a18&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3fca252d&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/recording-playback-and-smart-motion-search#video-player-user-interface)

Video Player User Interface


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FNFGb9l6qxrUW97e61qhV%252FGroup%252019.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa2a20cd-0fba-4b48-9c8b-1e8ce49403a9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e4514e63&sv=2)

1.  **FullScreen: click to have fullscreen of the videos.**
    
2.  **Camera detail:** Go to the camera detail page to adjust camera settings.
    
3.  **Share URL**: Anyone who has the URL can access it without authentication. The video is not autoplay to be able to have audio when playing. It is easy to share an abnormal event with a person who has no EeGenius account, like police.
    
4.  **Audio On/Off:** Enable/Disable microphone of camera to pick up remote audio.
    
5.  **Export Video:** Trim video from start time to end time on timeline
    
6.  **Snapshot**: Directly have a snapshot at that moment when you click the button.
    
7.  **Previous/Next Event**: Quickly navigate through recorded events in the camera's playback timeline.
    
8.  **Stop at previous/next frame**: Precisely navigate through recorded footage frame by frame. This is especially useful for detailed analysis or capturing specific moments in the footage.
    
9.  **Play/pause video**: click to switch to play or stop video and adjust the volume.
    
10.  Play speed: This allows you to adjust the play speed. If you play at higher speed, you will get more footage frame from the cameras and double more throughputs.
    
11.  Digital Zoom: Adjust the zoom level and focus on specific areas of the camera's view using the mouse.
    
    *   **Scroll Up:** Zoom in to view details more closely.
        
    *   **Scroll Down:** Zoom out to expand the field of view.
        
    *   **Click and Drag:** After zooming in, click on the screen and drag to adjust the visible area within the zoomed-in frame.
        
    
12.  Adjust the timeline duration: Allows you to change the time line duration for the video time bar.
    
13.  Live icon: click to go to live view instantly.
    
14.  Calendar: Click to search the video footage at a specific day and time directly.
    

Last updated 4 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Camera AI settings | Cloud User Manual

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details/camera-ai-settings#camera-ai)

Camera AI


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

User can set for in-cam AI. There are 5 sensitivity levels for people and vehicles, respectively. By default, it is Medium. Lower sensitivity will have fewer video events.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FrK0OvSqZZiZyYVG23PEH%252F1735537414466.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D001fec7f-eb1d-40b4-8c90-2b51022861e6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cc98ed4e&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details/camera-ai-settings#undefined)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details/camera-ai-settings#cloud-ai)

Cloud AI


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, it is disabled. If enabled, people or vehicles could consume tokens to analyze their activities during the video frame. Note: Cloud AI can be enabled/disabled only if camera AI was enabled manually or by default. Cloud AI needs AI tokens to work. If AI tokens run out, video activity analysis will stop until AI tokens are recharged. Cloud AI events could depend on camera AI sensitivity since objects will be detected by camera AI and sent to cloud AI for advanced activity analysis.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FByDeNowX4l4V9C8EuQtu%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%259C%2596%25202025-07-03%2520%25E4%25B8%25AD%25E5%258D%258812.03.47.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0282423-551f-4905-a3fd-67a16fef06f7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b1e09e32&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details/camera-ai-settings#event-alert)

Event Alert

These event alerts will send email/App notifications after you enable alerts on each event.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FIYTSHjYgYelxHJbOBPKk%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%259C%2596%25202025-07-03%2520%25E4%25B8%258A%25E5%258D%258811.59.13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77d72561-63c3-4f73-ba58-16702791e53e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4a4232e2&sv=2)

Event alert will also appear in the bell icon

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FvoXtOpImRvsz3wolwRL8%252F1737524474442.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c64f043-f076-4f1f-82dc-9ec27c7737cd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4952e658&sv=2)

Email Notification needs to be enabled; otherwise, alerts won't take effect.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FYKVl6FNa9j8Olb5BS7eT%252F1735614025690.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd1f3b34c-362f-4959-982d-2dcbaccb8c06&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b251b44&sv=2)

Notification settings page

Cross-line counting Alerts need to be added to the cross-line by clicking **Edit line** action

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252Frpc2mvYUmgZG8NizlF4m%252F1735611772365.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77849903-e7ed-45b6-bf83-75aa9fca4d5c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d2ff9438&sv=2)

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FUiPmLhMQyKacjVU9qxd7%252F1735612741285.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4de723d-73dd-468b-a415-e99bb9ae4f5b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e9d0f307&sv=2)

Cross-Line editing page

Region Counting Alert needs to be added to the cross-region by clicking the **Edit Region** action and assigning the people/vehicles that show up in any region.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F8jhRDgyARmxdtiezWL0r%252F1735612930019.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D84586976-588c-4dcf-83d8-202e7f524dca&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=63b692aa&sv=2)

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FM6fpKWpfnGZVK9W06gDL%252F1735612786641.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44d40c3b-c8be-4008-9571-faaafb739da2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3791c6da&sv=2)

Region Editing page

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details/camera-ai-settings#schedule)

Schedule


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is the schedule that controls when to send the AI notification to the user, which will consume the AI Point as well. Camera AI handles detection, while other features like Camera AI Alerts, Cloud AI analysis, and Cloud AI Alerts follow the schedule. This allows for managing alert schedules and Cloud AI costs.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F3vgOITQCi1I6JrJNj7Of%252F1735549950605.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4baaaf4f-eb95-494c-86c9-7a38dad3d112&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=67a99add&sv=2)

# Video Walls | Cloud User Manual

Video walls are for security to do daily monitoring of the cameras’ live video. It can be used on multiple displays through all cameras.

you can access this screen **Manage** > **Camera** > **Video walls**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FX1sGXZGraFTZzHO5LnMF%252F1735614725063.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50a17879-f709-4ce5-9cef-a5f4483c0589&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4492dbb0&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/video-walls#add-video-walls)

Add Video Walls


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F8adPKPW7vhD7RhA1Emr6%252F1724659890968.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19cade5c-b6ee-47de-9d27-374406b0a303&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c135ec01&sv=2)

**Auto-create TV wall**: Cameras remaining that are not on the existing TV wall will be added in order of camera name. They are put into the selected layout from top to bottom and left to right. TV walls and their names are generated automatically until all remaining cameras are added. The 4x4 layout is used in most situations, and this way saves a lot of setting time. Other layouts (3x3) and more tiles are optional for users to select.

**Name** : the video walls name

**Layout**: the video wall layout allows you to put the camera inside it.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/video-walls#edit-video-walls)

Edit Video Walls


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After you create the video layouts, you can click **Edit** button to edit video walls details

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F9p5xdZVmHLBmEyGygoar%252F1735614857066.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df57d9976-06ca-4036-a85e-33b574f3e2f0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a037de87&sv=2)

Then click Add cameras button

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FYpumPLRiobkSkoNNhFYp%252F1725003702020.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7857889-cdc3-456b-96e7-237de104ebac&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=455dcd72&sv=2)

**Better to know**

*   Video wall must be composed of cameras within the same network. cameras on different networks should be set up in separate video walls.
    
*   Same camera could be added to multiple video walls, but same camera can only appear once on the same video wall.
    

Then drag the cameras inside the Video walls , then click **Apply**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252Fcl9m392cOSpNfsyhfOtE%252F1725004519790.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbfcd92c8-162c-4449-bb0c-0f93bf0ecb1a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=554166ad&sv=2)

# Configure and Check Camera Details | Cloud User Manual

For each camera, there are more settings available to configure and fine-tune the system. In addition, EnGenius Cloud collects and aggregates lots of data reported by camera periodically. Sophisticated graphs and tables are available on the camera detail page to ease the monitoring and tracking of a camera. To get all the details, on **the cameras** page, hover your mouse cursor on the row of cameras you are interested in. A **Details** button is shown, and click on it to get into the camera detail page. To reboot cameras, you can still hover on the row of cameras. and click on the **Reboot** button.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F2eTLLPiCLPqKWBf7WPqg%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%259C%2596%25202025-07-08%2520%25E4%25B8%258A%25E5%258D%258810.04.36.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D32e2c0cf-e6b5-4568-a860-4523e1b0936b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e92072c&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details#summary)

Summary


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The first TAB page summarizes the camera's current settings and states. All details of configurations and statistics are shown on this page. On the top of the page, you can find the LED blinking button; this is used when you want to find where the camera is.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FuLEHFuU1TjZHAAEDaK01%252F1736759003927.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D98686701-3268-40e5-8eb4-59b4ef6dfedd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fb63e95b&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details#people-vehicle-activities)

**People / Vehicle Activities**

People and Vehicle Counting help you to gain valuable insights into the number of people or vehicles that appear in a particular location.

This data can then be used to gain a better understanding of the traffic flow and density of persons or vehicles in the area, allowing for informed decision-making and better security planning

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FMmP9uBZq0r69mpDj7lP2%252F1733809802847.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db1680637-75e6-44d6-af70-ec8d3d1a8712&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=492deb&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details#record-overview)

Record Overview

The will display whether the camera was recording video or not over a period of time. Green bars indicate the camera was recording on that period of time , The gray bar means the camera is not recording on that period of time

Place your cursor over each bar to see date, time, and recording status.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FUSgpyVeqdCi33jVnx8cR%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%259C%2596%25202024-09-02%2520%25E4%25B8%258B%25E5%258D%25885.03.56.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf0ba31c-9093-4c19-8f52-e37b8d8fee4b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a8aec91&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details#traffic)

Traffic

Traffic shows the camera Tx and Rx over a period of time

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FlonIQMF4mBJYbjmZ1KjU%252F1725269081328%25402x.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe0362bf-1639-4585-a36c-ea7d55937924&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1cb5993a&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details#camera-settings)

Camera settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FynZLBjDynsdbmnVEXeW6%252F1725874496022.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dda5874dd-d907-4bd0-89e3-8a906e29f16f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b85de7dd&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details#image-control)

Image Control

*   **Brightness**: Adjust the brightness level of the camera feed using the slider. The range is from 0% (minimum brightness) to 100% (maximum brightness). Increase the percentage to brighten the image, useful for low-light environments.
    
*   **Contrast**: Modify the contrast level to enhance differences between light and dark areas in the image. Use the slider to set a value between 0% (lowest contrast) and 100% (highest contrast).
    

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details#day-night-mode)

Day night Mode

Select the operating mode for the camera based on lighting conditions:

*   **Auto**: Automatically switches between day and night mode based on ambient light levels.
    
*   **Always Day**: Keeps the camera in day mode regardless of lighting conditions, ideal for well-lit environments.
    
*   **Always Night**: forces the camera into night mode, useful for consistently dark areas or nighttime surveillance.
    

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details#orientation)

Orientation

Adjust the orientation of the camera image:

*   **Normal**: Standard orientation, suitable for most setups.
    
*   **Upside Down**: Flips the image vertically and mirror it too. Use this setting when the camera is mounted upside down.
    

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details#iris-mode)

Iris Mode

**Iris** refers to the adjustable aperture of the camera lens that regulates the amount of light entering the camera sensor. Proper adjustment of the Iris ensures optimal image quality in varying lighting conditions.

Iris settings are critical to avoid issues like **flickering**, **rolling effects**, or over/underexposed images, depending on the environment where the camera is installed.

*   Fixed Mode: The Iris is set to its **maximum opening**, allowing the maximum amount of light to enter the sensor. Suitable for low-light environments where capturing as much light as possible is essential.
    
*   Indoor: Prioritizes eliminating **flickering** and **rolling effects** caused by indoor artificial lighting.
    
*   Outdoor: Auto-setting Iris to get best quality, but easy to meet rolling or flicker effect in indoor environment.
    

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details#high-dynamic-range)

High Dynamic Range

High dynamic range are camera techniques for capturing the same image at different exposures and then merging those images together to form a single image. This is particularly useful where the image consists of very light and very dark areas (e.g., an indoor camera that faces a window to outside).

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details#privacy-mask)

Privacy Mask

Privacy Mask allows you to block sensitive areas from a camera’s feed. After you apply a privacy window to an area of the camera feed, subsequent video in the specified area is covered by dark.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/configure-and-check-camera-details#real-time-steaming-protocol)

Real-Time Steaming Protocol

RTSP streaming is for 3rd party applications, NVR, VMS, or NAS. Both live video and audio are streamed out at the same time.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FW6hST7M69DzW7WfNGJIe%252F1733732752604.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db8d43796-b39c-4106-b005-f43af3d4500c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5336c938&sv=2)

1.  Username/password : 3rd party application client needs them for Digest authentication during connection.
    
2.  High Resolution URL: This is created automatically for copying to clipboard and being pasted in 3rd party applications.
    

Last updated 1 day ago

Was this helpful?

Flash (0.5 sec interval)

Mesh Backbone Weak

Blue

Orange

# Default SSIDs | Cloud User Manual

**Default SSIDs (only available before ECW AP is managed by EnGenius Cloud)**

Potential known default SSID names along with potential causes/solutions:

**EnMGMTxxxx-Initializing**

Cause: AP is in bootup sequence.

**EnMGMTxxxx-SSID\_name>-No\_Eth**

Cause: AP does not have an Ethernet connection.

Solution: Check if the Ethernet cable is unplugged.

**EnMGMTxxxx-No\_IP**

Cause: AP cannot get an IP address from the DHCP server. Solution: Check the AP's IP address configuration.

**EnMGMTxxxx-IP\_Conflict**

Cause: AP’s IP address conflicts with another device’s IP in the same network.

Solution: Check the AP's IP address configuration.

**EnMGMTxxxx-Gateway\_ERR**

Cause: AP is unable to connect to its default gateway.

Solution: Check the AP's IP address configuration and connectivity to its default gateway.

**EnMGMTxxxx-Proxy\_ERR**

Cause: AP could not access Internet through an HTTP/HTTPS proxy.

Solution: Check the AP’s proxy configuration in Miscellaneous Settings.

**EnMGMTxxxx-DNS\_ERR**

Cause: AP could not resolve the domain name from the DNS server.

Solution: Check the AP's IP address configuration.

**EnMGMTxxxx-Cloud\_ERR**

Cause: Everything appears to work normally, but device is unable to connect to cloud server.

Solution: Check cloud server status with EnGenius.

**EnMGMTxxxx-No\_Cloud\_Configure**

Cause: AP’s S/N has not been added to any network.

Solution: Check whether the AP has been added in the inventory and has been added to a network.

**EnMGMTxxxx-Cloud\_Configured**

Everything is working as it should!

**EnMGMTxxxx**

Cause: An AP has never connected to the EnGenius cloud or has been factory reset.

Last updated 5 years ago

Was this helpful?

---

# VPN Status | Cloud User Manual

This page will show you the VPN status of the Gateway in relation to all other EnGenius Gateways or Non-EnGenius Gateways in your organization with site-to-site VPN enabled**.** You can access the VPN Status page by navigating to **Manage > VPN Status.**

If you are in the Organization scope, you could select the gateway to monitor the current VPN status in relation to other EnGenius Peers or NonEnGenius Peers by switching the tab

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FQJyLFXpE4Bc10ebhZnYP%252F1656655248494.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3cbb4edd-012a-444e-8513-740fa7271500&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ad372847&sv=2)

Under the **EnGenius Peers** tab, the following information is available

*   Gateway: The name of the EnGenius Gateway.
    
*   Network: The Network to which the gateway is assigned.
    
*   WAN IP: The WAN IP of the remote gateway.
    
*   Subnet: The remote subnet network address behind the remote gateway that can be reached through Site to Site VPN.
    
*   Type: The type that is configured on the Configure > Gateway > Site to Site VPN
    
*   Usage: The amount of traffic to and from that EnGenius VPN peer.
    
*   Latency: Round-trip time latency between the EnGenius Gateway and the remote peers.
    
*   Uptime: This shows the time that the VPN tunnel has been active
    

If You are in the Network scope, it will display the gateway in the network to monitor the current VPN status in relation to other EnGenius Peers or NonEnGenius Peers.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FmihWdGJb1dfJzWEHd1ID%252F1656658229029.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9870b49e-f40a-4edb-927d-4aefdaedf4df&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebf106e&sv=2)

On the **non-EnGenius peer's** tab, the following information is available

*   **Gateway:** Name of the EnGenius Gateway.
    
*   **WAN IP:** The WAN IP is configured for the non-EnGenius peer.
    
*   **Subnet:** The remote subnet network address behind the remote non-EnGenius gateway that can be reached through Site to Site VPN.
    

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-gateway/vpn-status#vpn-map)

VPN Map


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users can drag & drop EnGenius Gateway and Non-EnGenius Gateway in the Organization to Google Maps and have a holistic view of the gateway deployed on google Maps and see the VPN topology. You can access this page **Manage** > **VPN Status** > **Map**

the color will show the latency of the VPN link to let the user has a quick view of the quality of each VPN link.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F6DIaCRsOebfbZeuksKaR%252F1669689645438.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80674661-3972-45f6-ada6-5d42de165184&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=832915b2&sv=2)
