# Configure and Check Gateway Details | Cloud User Manual

For each Gateway, EnGenius Cloud collects and aggregates lots of data reported by the Gateway periodically. Sophisticated graphs and tables are available on the gateway detail page to ease the monitoring and tracking of a gateway. To get all the details, on the **Gateway** page, hover your mouse cursor on the row of Gateway you are interested in. A **Detail** button is shown click on it to get into the Gateway detail page.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FARJ6JgHmSUdkAVAL01MS%252F1656558326328.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddc7af111-ade7-4a6b-b260-0226fff7d868&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba289c14&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-gateway/configure-and-check-gateway-details#wan)

WAN


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This will display the WAN Info that you configured in the **Configure > Gateway > Interface > WAN**

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-gateway/configure-and-check-gateway-details#wan-info)

WAN Info

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F16AiBfrIkXaIJbRAaVzv%252F1656557134241.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc5dea3a2-bfaa-4bc0-be96-4c8a42dfcc4c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f444856b&sv=2)

*   **Interface:** Display WAN1 or WAN2
    
*   **Name:** The name of WAN1 or WAN2
    
*   **Connection:** DHCP, PPPoE, or Static
    
*   **Public IP:** This is the Internet public IP address of the WAN interface seen by the EnGenius Cloud. If there is an upstream NAT device, then this is the public IP address of the NAT device. If the gateway WAN interface is directly connected to the Internet, then this is the native IP address of the WAN interface.
    
*   **WAN IP:** The native IP address of the WAN interface. If the WAN interface is directly connected to the Internet, then this IP address is the same as the **Public IP**. If the WAN interface is connected to an upstream NAT device, then this IP address is usually a private IP address.
    
*   **Gateway:** the Gateway IP address of the WAN interface which is used as the next-hop gateway for Internet access through this WAN interface.
    

**Good to know**

The status bar near the WAN1/WAN2, Green means that this Interface has an internet connection, and Grey means this interface has no internet connection.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-gateway/configure-and-check-gateway-details#latency)

Latency

This graph shows the Latency between the EnGenius Security Gateway and Google Public DNS in a day/week/month view. Hover and click Day/Week/Month to see the latency graph view by Day/Week/Month.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FAoC2wIJt71xr2JVylu8F%252F1656482286380.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74838df2-ca9e-4304-ac51-17794067c24e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c288cfdc&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-gateway/configure-and-check-gateway-details#lan)

LAN


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The LAN tab displays the following information.

*   **LAN Interface**: the name of the LAN Interface
    
*   **Subnet**: the subnet IP address of the LAN Interface of the gateway
    
*   **Used**: the number of leased DHCP IP addresses of the gateway DHCP server for this LAN interface
    
*   **Free**: the number of remaining leasable DHCP IP addresses of the gateway DHCP server for this LAN interface
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FUWVDaAQYyDzaoCFvaUYa%252F1656556797999.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D986fde74-ec43-4c5e-98f2-53e7d9e7d32e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9e2c3f3&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-gateway/configure-and-check-gateway-details#dhcp-lease)

DHCP Lease


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The DHCP Lease tab shows the current DHCP leasing status of the gateway. The following information is displayed.

*   **Client**: the name of the DHCP client
    
*   **MAC**: the MAC address of the DHCP client
    
*   **IP**: the DHCP IP address of the DHCP client
    
*   **LAN Interface**: the LAN interface that the DHCP client was connected to
    
*   **Expires in**: the expiration time of the leased DHCP IP address
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F7V7JXEvo8VI8WVA1087s%252F1656473113863.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc7c72b9-bf94-46e9-ac5c-8335f2897a97&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=34458192&sv=2)

The following clients **will not** appear in the DHCP leases table:

*   Clients with statically assigned addresses
    
*   Clients with fixed DHCP assignments
    
*   Clients receiving an address from another DHCP server
    
*   Clients that have not successfully received an address from the EnGenius Gateway
    
*   Clients connected over the client VPN
    

Last updated 10 months ago

Was this helpful?

# AI-Powered Search | Cloud User Manual

AI-Powered Search allows users to search by inputting natural and multiple languages in the free description form of a search bar, like they do on Google Search. Query is compared with camera metadata in the database across multiple cameras in an organization and ranking results in order. The user can explore result snapshots and play video clips of them

You can find the search bar from **Manage > Cameras**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FapmbhnzkvOh442bkFRnT%252F1734420159873.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D199a23b3-350a-479f-a666-627252a2e6d7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=45f59a16&sv=2)

Search results could be ranked in an order from top to bottom and left to right based on most relevant. Most relevant is the highest comparison score between the user query and camera metadata. Click on one of the result thumbnails to play a video clip of 15 seconds since the start time of the event. Clear search input to go back to camera list.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FjpfJ7yoafWwB18oa2VNi%252F1735614659962.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D113e1558-8412-4cca-9096-cec91997db03&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5a04474a&sv=2)

**Must know**

*   Camera PRO license is required to active AI search
    
*   Enable Cloud AI settings of a camera to generate metadata of video activity analysis for AI search. Camera enabled camera ai cannot generate meta data for AI search.
    

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-camera/ai-powered-search#add-sd-alert)

Add SD Alert


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After users see the search result and want to get the alerts from the condition, you can add the condition to the SD Alert.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FpZhVTimaFKY0nL2KKObn%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%259C%2596%25202025-06-17%2520%25E4%25B8%258B%25E5%258D%25885.44.58.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb4984dc-6cc7-4bc8-afc5-d47a27763c5b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8c071b2d&sv=2)

# Managing Access Points | Cloud User Manual

Once you created Orgs and Networks to define the scope of managed networks, next step is to add the devices to the managed network and manage them. To manage the Access Points in a Network, trigger the toolbar menu at the left-hand side: **Manage > Access Points**.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point#add-an-ap-to-network)

Add an AP to Network


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on **Add from Inventory button.** You can then pick the devices registered to the Org previously and add them to current Network.

**Must Know**:

One device can only be added to one network. All devices in the same network should apply the same network-wide settings except the settings are overridden individually.

**Tips**:

when you have multiple Org/Networks, you can stay in the AP list page and directly change the scope of Org/Networks. The system would lead you to different AP list pages quickly.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point#quickview-panel)

Quickview Panel


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Single click on the row of a AP (anywhere but hyperlink). It invokes a Quickview Panel that helps showing important status and key configurations for you. User can quickly finetune settings and do comparisons among different APs without going in and out different pages.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lkb97xKfXGwTDCqgBFb%252F-Lkb9BgYgDoASRZ5TfDt%252F1564025043113.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6cf384d0-b5de-4b0d-ba27-78258d3fec68&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c409bbff&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point#customize-radio-settings)

Customize Radio Settings

It's pretty common that for some cases you need to set channel or Tx power for specific APs. This would require the capability to override network's default radio settings.

Follow these steps to customize the radio settings for an AP.

1.  Choose an access point from the list to show its expanded settings.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LnLjW7vkG-VjS2CMOSl%252F-LnLjbHM5anQtpN6JDq0%252F1566970845775.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D21855f5f-1f0a-4b97-b8da-4f704427516a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=da791dc6&sv=2)

2\. In the **Radio** section, click the checkbox below the lock icon to override default settings.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LnLjW7vkG-VjS2CMOSl%252F-LnLk_sIK8YuQ9Wkkx8n%252F1566971120780.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd483d0a8-3180-47f7-889a-d5657f940172&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7d51254&sv=2)

3.Configure the following settings for both the 2.4GHz and 5GHz radio band:

*   Channel
    
*   Tx Power
    
*   Channel Width
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LnLkvKawIepfzVbyI57%252F-LnLkydovo5USmYZij-4%252F1566971223755.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee7c8b36-c7e7-43f3-893f-a05e2967bb8e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=39b34452&sv=2)

4\. Click **Apply.**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LnLkvKawIepfzVbyI57%252F-LnLl1nPV0UbyUPJRxjA%252F1566971235046.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D08262c91-6bbd-42c6-9f4b-d4aa2cfeb703&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba54276&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point#customize-ssid-settings)

Customize SSID settings

Although APs in the same network share the same SSID settings, sometimes you just do not want a specific AP to enable all SSIDs in the network. For example, you don't want the SSID of financial department to be enabled and accessible everywhere. In the [Quickview Panel](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point#ap-quickview-panel)
, you can also finetune and override SSID settings.

Follow the steps to override network-wide settings and enable or hide the SSID of a network.

1\. In the **WLAN** section, click on the checkbox near lock icon to override default settings.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LnLnZsdQ-GIJvKM8A4T%252F-LnLneKqhb0draUxK7FT%252F1566971824097.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc5b71ea0-4d08-4c91-a3d1-a04dd9d9f813&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5a3f8d0c&sv=2)

2\. Configure SSID to be enabled or hidden per your request.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LnLnt6M_3LFalG5cEV5%252F-LnLoFC5wkjcKidh0g5v%252F1566972090285.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df222dde9-bd8d-4ed9-93af-0f3ebbb4309e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1cd03f0c&sv=2)

3\. Click **Apply.**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LnLoJSuuhOjDgYoomUu%252F-LnLoVxsOPI32F8XaG4M%252F1566972168302.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da58c102e-4d9e-429d-afb2-ad5c18194404&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d75d5b8&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point#manipulate-aps-in-a-network)

Manipulate APs in a Network


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you have APs added to the network, you can apply more actions on the APs:

*   Move
    
    Select one or multiple access points and click to move the AP(s) to another hierarchy view/network.
    
*   Remove
    
    Select one or multiple access points and click to remove from the current org/hierarchy view/network.
    

Last updated 11 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Diag Tools | Cloud User Manual

This allows you to run the diagnostic tests that can help the Network administrator to troubleshoot.

Under AP detail page > you can easily see the “Diag Tools” icon

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FIjphLzD5gFxSUg6mvaqN%252F1638945626276.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfcea211a-1285-4a3c-b489-de70561efe7b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c8699c5&sv=2)

Under Manage > Access Points > Diag

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FJ3ybNH1BY9Xxv2lkaVyB%252F1638954254957.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ab2148b-2ab2-440c-a92e-0709e56e6ae3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=244ac929&sv=2)

So the Full-screen tools are displayed, So you can use them.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FQU4bFGCXQGWZfFKc6Qwe%252F1638954607107.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db188b5e8-9e37-4371-a038-879afa06dcce&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f393db1a&sv=2)

*   Diag Tools are all “real-time”
    
*   AP diagnostic tools includes (1) Activity: CPU/Memory/Throughput/Channel Utilization(2) Speed test / Ping (3) traceroute (4) All channel utilization (5) Live Clients + (6) Spectrum Analyzer
    
*   Except Spectrum Analyzer is for “S” models only, (1)-(5) are all available for all models
    
*   Activity: The info is as now and we add “non-WiFi” channel utilization % to let users know how much of the total channel utilization rate is from non-WiFi, so users can know if the interfering is from other AP or the environment of the channel is dirty and got high white noise.
    
*   For the Speed test, users can choose one from the “Test Server” list (detected by AP) and do a speed test, so when users have an issue on “slow connectivity” issue, the admin can check if it’s due to “Slow uplink” of AP or due to dirty WiFi between client and AP.
    
*   Ping: We put 3 default servers for users to check the latency change. User can also define their own server for the ping test.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FRQjf7s5vFuQB584Gleyq%252F1638955105906.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d36b4f4-6cf5-48b4-b7dc-23119913cdd4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5f018267&sv=2)

*   Traceroute: By default, we set the destination site to Google for the traceroute, and max hop is set to 8, which can be changed by the user. Traceroute allows user to know “the path” from the AP to the destination and will list every router/gateway (hop) and its latency, so if the destination is unreachable, then there must be some setting issue on router/gateway; and from the latency of each hop, the user will know the “slow uplink” is caused by which router/gateway. When the latency is over 10ms, the color will change to yellow, and if > 40ms, the color will change to red.
    
*   All channel utilization: This is a useful tool that user can easily see how dirty each channel is at a glance, and decide if he wants to change the channel of the AP manually. “Green” is “WiFi” traffic and “Orange” is “non-WiFi” interfering. By mouse-over, you can see the details of how much the % of WiFi and non-WiFi.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FPX395MxO0ZfaNLJcXhUl%252F1638955635826.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4b64b796-c6ad-4157-bede-d0a9f24e4c90&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d712be69&sv=2)

*   For the spectrum analysis tool (spectrogram or waterfall graph), we provide a rolling timeline view of signal strengths measured. The upper part shows the signal strength (RSSI) detected and the color indicates how many sources have been detected. The Lower part is the timeline view to let users know that, for example, channel 8 is dirtier than others, which might not be able to show from glance view of all channel utilization at the time, because the interfering source might not emit continuously but in high frequency.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FQtvPxhFLRsMTVPMzkhgu%252F1638861992646.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1da74fff-9b71-45b2-ae46-5018ffa10865&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c1ae6aea&sv=2)

In the Live clients, you can monitor the clients that are connected to specific AP. You can use it when the AP feature plan is PRO.

In the AP Basic feature plan, we only allow you to use the Diag tool in 1 min, after 1 min, Diag tools will be deactivated. If you want to use it longer, you can switch the AP feature plan to PRO.

you can use the diag tool when the AP firmware is 1.x.35 or above.

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Configure and Check AP Details | Cloud User Manual

For each AP, there are more settings available to configure and fine-tune the system. In addition, EnGenius Cloud collects and aggregates lots of data reported by AP periodically. Sophisticated graphs and tables are available on the AP detail page to ease the monitoring and tracking of an AP. To get all the details, on **AP list** page, hover your mouse cursor on the row of AP you are interested in. A **Details** button is shown and clicks on it to get into AP detail page.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LkbAFPmvC3G1s5BOcWG%252F-LkbAlV7G2R052OtZcaE%252F1564025473137.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db3f73278-3068-44ea-9a5f-2299f148468c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1fe00b99&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#summary)

Summary


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The first TAB page summarizes AP's current settings and states. All details of configurations and statistics are shown on this page.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#ssid)

SSID

The SSID section allows you to check and configure the exact SSID settings for this AP.

*   **SSID**: shows the SSID name.
    
*   **Radio**: shows the Radio (2.4GHz or 5GHz bands) turned on in this AP.
    
*   **Security**: security type set on the SSID.
    
*   **Captive portal**: shows authentication type for captive portal.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LnLv6P80BPjYRgt6NSP%252F-LnLvB0YAnXcwOnuMSDV%252F1566973781112.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d9af39d-d2d8-49ce-a4f3-bcb450a84162&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=68760ba2&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#throughput)

**Throughput**

The Throughput section allows you to check the throughput statistics for this AP. Note that you can control the filters to get different results based on your requirement:

*   By SSID
    
*   By Time (daily/weekly/monthly)
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LnLxI8obZMiT0QCqxeY%252F-LnLxLWPj_rTra1BOO2k%252F1566974472168.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29921a4c-6c4a-448f-b94e-bb48a19a8857&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a64abcde&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#radio)

**Radio**

The Radio section allows you to configure individual radio settings. The default radio setting will be followed by the network radio setting. If you want the radio settings of an access point to be different from the default, you can override them with custom values.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LlFlpMb3X4raARBXRLI%252F-LlFm6H0VB7aHmIddk88%252F1564723310547.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D843eace2-85a0-4948-b1b3-30f11d85f96a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d32d1cbe&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#fast-handover)

**Fast Handover**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enables customization of RSSI thresholds for specific APs to address unique scenarios. This will override the settings located on **Configure Radios > Fast Handover**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FsUrYmr6bmD74T2ehOIoH%252F1736227217745.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db8911d8e-51b9-4510-b1bf-b6e86641e489&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8c4bac&sv=2)

This requires AP Firmware V1.X.82 or later version.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#ip-addressing)

**IP Addressing**

This section allows you to configure IP address settings for the AP individually.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F1XAW444wsh0grvOzdN5D%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da48b2898-65da-43af-a2ea-817adbea5501&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=529a0b3a&sv=2)

*   **DHCP**: You can choose to auto assign IP addresses if there is a **DHCP** server in the network.
    
*   **Static:** Allows you to manually assign an IP address.
    
    Enter the IP address you wish to assign to the access point and fill in the subnet mask, default gateway, and DNS server address.
    
*   **IPV4 Address**: Enter the IP address for the access point.
    
*   **Subnet Mask**: Enter the subnet mask for the access point.
    
*   **Gateway**: Enter the default gateway for the access point.
    
*   **DNS Server 1**: Enter the primary DNS server name.
    
*   **DNS Server 2:** Enter the secondary DNS server name.
    

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#photos)

Photos

When an AP is just installed, you can take a photo (or several) on the AP and uploaded it to EnGenius Cloud as a property data for the AP. It's helpful for the installer to memorize where and how he installed the AP.

**Good to Know**: It is easier to take photo and upload it in Cloud-to-go App.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#logs)

Logs


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The EnGenius Cloud Log contains several logging subsystems that each have unique data retention and export options available. Datasets like device event, system configuration, and analytics are used for starkly different purposes (business intelligence, operations, risk management, etc.) and are reflected in the native logging capabilities. In the Log TAB page, the system list all the device logs for current AP. If you need to track events across a network, check [Device Events](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/analytics/device-events)
 for more details.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LkcOewwuBRmxqRQh-Gt%252F-LkcOnSbeOdXsAoIppeW%252F1564045901734.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3def09ef-c1da-42ba-abb2-b5caf5041eb4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9c6dfed1&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#filtering)

Filtering

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F4HfxrsO4F1ldhixBkLqp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6f205f2-80e6-4236-9cf8-139ed2d551bd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17a9c4d1&sv=2)

Log Filter

While the device log provides a thorough timeline of events on the AP, it is usually unnecessary to view all events. The following options are available to filter down the event log as needed.

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#filtering-by-ssid-or-client)

Filtering By SSID or Client

Filtering events to a specific client can help troubleshoot individual connectivity issues. Entering the MAC address, hostname, or custom name in the **Client** field will display only events affecting that client, excluding other client information and device events. For the same reason, **SSID** field can be used to filter out events related with other SSIDs.

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#filtering-by-date-and-time)

Filtering By Date and Time

The event log shows all events for clients and devices, starting with the most recent event by default. The date and time filters are useful to display only events that happened at or before the specified time.

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#filtering-by-severity)

Filtering By Severity

The event log are categorized in different severity:

*   Error
    
*   Warning
    
*   General
    

You can also set the filter to only show the logs with dedicated severity.

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#filtering-by-event-type)

Filtering By Event Type

The following types of events will be reported by ECW access points:

*   WLAN Client Connection
    
*   WLAN Client Control
    
*   WLAN Radio
    
*   Client Roaming
    
*   Device Status
    
*   Mesh
    
*   AirGuard
    

The filter also support all types of events listed above.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#clients)

Clients


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Clients** page provides comprehensive details of wireless clients that ever managed by the access point.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FPYvU7CYHk9Y295rK61yn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5802c609-c023-4e6b-a856-c737e16f7fb9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4ac20b5a&sv=2)

This page is filtered for current AP and supports all features as same as in [Managing Clients](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-clients)
. To get more details, please refer to the [Managing Clients](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-clients)
 section.

**Tips**:

*   To browse the clients page by page, you just need to scroll down the page to the end of screen. The web system will automatically load next page for you.
    
*   The clients in the list are historical data reported by AP minutes ago. If you want to see clients connecting with AP in realtime, click on the **Live Clients** link. It will lead you to the diag tools which give you an update of client list in seconds.
    

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#realtime-diagnostics)

Realtime Diagnostics


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

EnGenius Cloud provides powerful diag tools to track every details of your network in **REALTIME**. To trigger the Diag Tools, simply click on the diag button shown below:

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252Fkyd3QiluhnspHa6wcwuu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df66660e1-7d9a-44e9-85b1-3a188ad33411&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5ede1d1&sv=2)

Please refer to [Diag Tools](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diag-tools)
 to get more details.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#led-control)

LED Control


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the top of AP detail page, the are two buttons available to control AP LEDs instantly.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FZa787WKtsxEzrAXpcjgm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dabdad612-3e50-4d59-930a-463867a0fe13&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4bfeabc1&sv=2)

*   **LED Light**: This allows you to enable or disable all LEDs on the AP. This is helpful if users does not want to LEDs of AP interfering their vision at night.
    
*   **LED Blinking:** Click light bulb icon. LEDs on the AP will blink for 10 seconds. This helps the installer to find and identify a AP.
    

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/diagnosing-an-access-point#undefined)

# Terminology | EnGenius Cloud Licensing

EnGenius Cloud includes network hardware devices and a cloud platform, consisting of two essential components: an “Organization” and a “Network.” The following defined terms are used in this License Agreement.

Term

Description

**Associate**

Associate means to bind a License to a specific device.

**Associated Device**

A device with at least one associated License.

**License (or “Device License")**

One unit of usage rights granted to you and which can only be associated to one and only one device.

**License Activation Date**

The date on which a Device License commences, and thereby begins the licensing term.

**License Key**

A unique passcode (key) that a subscriber receives after the order is placed. A License Key may comprise multiple units of License of the same License model.

**License Issued Date**

The date that a license key is issued.

**Org Feature Plan**

The feature set available under different feature plans, including but not limited to a Basic Plan and a Pro plan, in the Organization.

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-overview/terminology#undefined)

Last updated 1 year ago

# License Activation | EnGenius Cloud Licensing

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-overview/license-activation#scenarios-to-activate-cloud-licenses)

Scenarios to activate Cloud licenses

Each EnGenius Cloud Pro license comes with a validity period (depends on the license type you purchased) and will remain active after being activated until it is expired.

There are two ways to activate a license

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3299519939-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MkFTP6mPDb3kJRwf2Rb%252Fuploads%252FwC9NmhJPVsprpNKj51rM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D764c120a-edd2-41c9-bdc6-ad10dbc2c483&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=89c95caa&sv=2)

Diagram 3 - Scenarios to activate Cloud licenses

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-overview/license-activation#manual-activation)

**Manual Activation**

**Associate licenses to the device and assign the device to a Network**

When you assign this license-associated device to any network in your organization, the license will start to activate and operate during its validity period. For example, Device A/B are assigned to Network 123 and 456, so AP-License 1 and 2 are activated from the date they are assigned to the Networks.

The license associated with the device will not be activated during the planning period **until the device is assigned to Network** and apply the configuration.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-overview/license-activation#forced-activation)

**Forced Activation**

**No license association or network assignment after 90 days of licenses issued**

Suppose you have never associated the license with any device, or the license-associated device has not been assigned to any managed network. In that case, this license will be automatically turned into an active state after it is issued for 90 days. _(Device C, diagram 3)_

After a license is forced activation, the validity period would start to burn. No matter the license is associated with a device or not.

Last updated 1 year ago

---

# License Order and License Key | EnGenius Cloud Licensing

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-overview/license-order-and-license-key#license-order-and-license-key-dispatch)

License order and license key dispatch

Partners purchase EnGenius Cloud licenses just like purchasing other hardware devices from EnGenius, except "delivery email list" information is required for the License Key to be mailed to. Once license P.O. is completed, the EnGenius license server will generate License Keys based on the order content and email to the recipients listed in the "delivery email list".

*   A purchase order (P.O.) contains multiple order lines.
    
*   One order line will generate one license key.
    
*   An Email list is mandatory in the License purchase order.
    
*   License key information (PDF) will be sent to the "delivery email list".
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3299519939-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MkFTP6mPDb3kJRwf2Rb%252Fuploads%252FL5tZBnj6IVaauiieNqVq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7bbde24-363b-4265-8847-7e646cf874b5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea4ec65&sv=2)

Lead time for license purchase order (P.O) should be within a few days. Suggest placing the license order whenever it's needed for deployment.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-overview/license-order-and-license-key#license-key-vs.-license)

License Key vs. License

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3299519939-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MkFTP6mPDb3kJRwf2Rb%252Fuploads%252FUX3KNKSNWWumUxyNQafD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd828b1bc-5e53-43b6-9a89-c86d8352b1f8&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=401de868&sv=2)

*   **License key** presents a group of Licenses (i.e. 4 units of AP-1YR-LIC)
    
*   _**One order line**_ from a PO (Purchase order) will generate _**one license key**_
    
*   When inserting _**License Key**_ into engenius cloud system, the _**License**_ is unzipped automatically. (there would be 4 licenses of AP-1YR-LIC extracted from one license key in this case).
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3299519939-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MkFTP6mPDb3kJRwf2Rb%252Fuploads%252FwQ4TsirX7LmvKiaPqDRU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db045200c-95ae-456d-818f-a31aee05b451&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=99536777&sv=2)

**License Key document** (PDF attached in email)

*   License key document (PDF) will be attached with the **license notification email**
    
*   PDF contains the purchased license model, quantity, validity period and its corresponding _**License Key**_.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3299519939-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MkFTP6mPDb3kJRwf2Rb%252Fuploads%252FujEXXPpmqhYntiTD7big%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df2a3fa69-0916-470d-9fc4-34ea08f9e026&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=892f1f3a&sv=2)

Last updated 1 year ago

# EnGenius Cloud Services DataCenters | Cloud White Papers

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/engenius-cloud-services-datacenters#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The EnGenius Cloud services are built upon fully redundant and highly available data centers with SSAE18 Type II audited and ISO27001 certifications. EnGenius Cloud architecture is a serverless design that functions and data are distributed across multiple redundant servers so that there is no single point of failure and every function module will scale by itself to reach high availability and high independency.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/engenius-cloud-services-datacenters#components)

Components

EnGenius Cloud is a distributed FaaS (Function-as-a-Service) design and the components include:

*   Cloud devices check-in service
    
*   End-user web GUI access service
    
*   Real-time monitoring service
    
*   End-user configuration database
    
*   Log and notification services
    
*   Services management center
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2788256466-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lo1AtG4HHv3uJq1FqqB%252Fuploads%252F2gM3tFlXCAaS7oOOrS61%252FFunction-as-a-Service.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4c08b59c-3a7c-4f90-9dc1-cdeec22f7217&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db271708&sv=2)

Figure01 -- Distributed Faas Design of EnGenius Cloud

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/engenius-cloud-services-datacenters#availability)

Availability

*   99.99% uptime service level agreement
    
*   24\*7 server health monitoring and report every 2 minutes
    
*   24\*7 automated failure detection test every 20 minutes
    
*   Rapid escalation procedures by multiple operation team shift
    

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/engenius-cloud-services-datacenters#redundancy)

Redundancy

*   Distributed Datacenters between multiple availability zones
    
*   Customer network configuration data and statistical data replicated across different zones
    
*   Real-time replication of data
    
*   Daily backups for network configuration, statistical data, and event logs
    

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/engenius-cloud-services-datacenters#disaster-recovery)

Disaster Recovery

*   Rapid failover to hot spare in event of hardware failure or natural disaster
    
*   The End-user network keeps running even if EnGenius Cloud connectivity is unreachable. (except the function of EnGenius Cloud Authentication)
    
    *   Users' data plane doesn't go through EnGenius Cloud
        
    *   Only Cloud devices' management plane goes through EnGenius Cloud for configuration and status reporting, so when the Cloud is not reachable, it won't impact the users' network normal operation and keep running.
        
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2788256466-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lo1AtG4HHv3uJq1FqqB%252Fuploads%252Fie7RzLTYt4Wq3GibgT1t%252FCloud%2520Authentication.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68c2bea2-4ac7-430c-8772-de7393678b1b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8c0cddd5&sv=2)

Figure02 -- Secured Cloud Management Platform

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/engenius-cloud-services-datacenters#secure-on-boarding-process)

Secure On-Boarding Process

*   Every Cloud device will have a unique certificate built-in from the factory
    
*   Cloud devices have to go through multiple-factory authentication (MFA) process to make sure the devices are legitimate devices, then the devices will have another private certificate from Cloud to build a secure tunnel between the devices and Cloud
    
*   Before the on-boarding, the device has to be registered in an Organization by the users
    
*   After the secure tunnel is built, the device starts to check in to the Cloud by sending the device information
    
*   If the device is assigned to a Network, then the Network configuration will be pushed to the device through the secure tunnel
    
*   The device will keep checking in to sync up the configuration and update device information
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2788256466-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lo1AtG4HHv3uJq1FqqB%252Fuploads%252FZZN5AmoMweSrEkQ1m67x%252FSecure%2520On-Boarding%2520Process.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7736cbb1-0f20-4249-82c9-2b7812563924&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4fb5331e&sv=2)

Figure03 -- Secure On-Boarding Process of EnGenius Cloud

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/engenius-cloud-services-datacenters#global-operation)

Global Operation

*   EnGenius builds team for Data Centers global operation to create several regional zones for back up whole FaaS services
    
*   For users to run global businesses, EnGenius Cloud infrastructure design allows users to manage different Networks under different Countries and timezones, so the firmware scheduling update time can be adoptive to local time and device operation mode can be compliant with local Country regulations such as available channels.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2788256466-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lo1AtG4HHv3uJq1FqqB%252Fuploads%252FwTmScdcyixJ3Tr9Yg4x7%252FGlobal%2520Operation.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc2322a96-843e-47e2-915d-30932b05d28c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7947d02a&sv=2)

Figure04 -- Global Operation with EnGenius Cloud

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/engenius-cloud-services-datacenters#service-security)

Service Security

*   24\*7 intrusion detection
    
*   Protected by IP and port-based firewalls
    
*   Administrator access with multiple-factor authentication enforcement
    
*   Remote access is restricted by IP address and authenticated using RSA-2048 public key
    
*   For communication between an EnGenius hardware device and the EnGenius cloud, EnGenius uses a lightweight encrypted tunnel with AES-256 encryption to secure management data in transit.
    

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/engenius-cloud-services-datacenters#infrastructure-security)

Infrastructure Security

*   All entries, exits of the datacenters are monitored by the surveillance camera
    
*   24\*7 security guards control all accesses into and out of datacenters to ensure only authorized persons can access the controlled zones with different privilege
    

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/engenius-cloud-services-datacenters#maintenance-process)

Maintenance Process

*   To keep improving the Cloud infrastructure and features, the operation team might need to upgrade the current production site
    
*   Any revision of code will do a full test at a staging site before pushing to the production site
    
*   Before the upgrade, the operation team will notify cloud users 2 days ago through a pop-up Post when users log in to Cloud to announce when the maintenance will be held and the estimated time of the action
    
*   During the maintenance window, users will be redirected to a maintenance window to let users know how long the maintenance will be. Since the data plane will not go through Cloud, so users' networks should still be functional
    
*   Users can also call local support to understand more details
    

Last updated 6 months ago

# Managing Switches | Cloud User Manual

Click **Manage > Switches** to access this screen and double-click the organization/hierarchy view/network on the tree to change the scope.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LiCfsrjpEQVK9xzmRqk%252F-LiCgAezftrMeM0e35qn%252FSwitch-24port%25402x%255B1%255D.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dafe8f3e8-e65b-49ba-8311-dcb85b5a35e9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5ce95dc2&sv=2)

The **Switch List** page lists all switches within your organization/hierarchy view/network, and allows you to choose each switch to view the port status, VLAN , STP and PoE.

The following describes the functions in this screen:

**Move to**: Select one or multiple switches and click to move the switches to another hierarchy view/network.

**Remove From Networks:** Select one or multiple switches and click to remove the switches from the current organization/hierarchy view/network.

**Add From Inventory:** Click this button to add switches from your existing inventory.

**Detail:** Click to display the individual switch details.

# AirGuard | Cloud User Manual

AirGuard is EnGenius technology to detect the rogue source, evil twins, DoS attacks, and RF jamming. You can access this screen under **Manage** \> **AirGuard**

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/airguard#rules)

Rules

1.  Users should **enable AirGuard** first (by default: off) to activate AP to detect the rogue source
    
2.  If Enabled "**Contain all Rogue Devices"**, all rogue SSID devices will be contained automatically and Zero-Wait DFS will not be functional.
    
3.  **Scanning APs** list down all APs who can do AirGuard (AirGuard AP), click “**Details**” will redirect to the AP detail page.
    
4.  Users can set rules to categorize specific SSID or BSSIDs with a **partial match** or **exact match**.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FEJhB8VZeqSafHr7Wtc8v%252F1679983848800.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb249c51-fca1-4276-9110-93ce4181f3e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=399bca5a&sv=2)

**Must know**

AirGuard requires at least one AP with dedicated scanning radio in this network. eg**,** ECW220S, ECW230S

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/airguard#rogue-ssid)

Rogue SSID


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   All SSID match “**Rogue rules**”
    
*   All SSID match legitimate SSID but are not recognized by Cloud-managed device (It could be rogue AP, it also could be other vendors' legitimate AP)
    
*   **Broadcast MACs** are the BSSID (MAC), detected by our AP, broadcasting the rogue SSID. It could be multiple BSSIDs. Click on the line to see detailed information.
    
*   **Seen by**: the Rogue SSID might be detected by multiple EnGenius AP
    
*   **Severity**: The rogue reason severity could be high and require the user’s attention. The color bar in front of the SSID indicates the severity: Very high: Red; High: Orange…
    
*   **Containment:** Contained means the rogue SSID that your EnGenius AP is currently containing. Whenever a client attempts to connect to the rogue SSID, they will be forced off. Uncontained means the Rogue SSID is not currently contained.
    
*   **Move to Whitelist**: If the user found the SSID should be legitimate, then he can select it and **move to whitelist** (move to “**Other SSIDs**”)
    
*   **Contain:** This is the action that if you determine the Rogue SSIDs are threats to your network, you could click contain so the client will be forced off when the client attempts to connect the Rogue SSIDs.
    
*   **Uncontain:** This is the action that the Rogue SSIDs were noticed during a scan, but has not been determined to be a threat to your network, so you could click Uncontain.
    
*   **More details:** [**https://docs.engenius.ai/whitepapers/airguard/rules-and-classifications#rogue-ssids**](https://docs.engenius.ai/whitepapers/airguard/rules-and-classifications#rogue-ssids)
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F5GT2Vq3jqO2XT06ic7Ss%252F1680772118832.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D769b07d9-2ee9-46f3-a674-c1745c1f9ae0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c90ead2a&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/airguard#evil-twin)

Evil Twin


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **AP impersonation**: SSID = legitimate SSID and BSSID = legitimate BSSID, which means someone is using the legitimate AP’s MAC and SSID trying to steal client information
    
*   **AP spoofing**: BSSID = legitimate BSSID, but not legitimate SSID
    
*   The severity is always “**Very High**” and requires attention.
    
*   **More details**: [https://docs.engenius.ai/whitepapers/airguard/evil-twin](https://docs.engenius.ai/whitepapers/airguard/evil-twin)
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252Fo6COK8i25gxWobrg4u4t%252F1649915167746.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ea981e6-f513-49fe-ba52-939a132a8587&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b281860d&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/airguard#malicious-attack)

Malicious Attack


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

DoS attack trying to let clients or specific clients not able to connect to the AP

*   **De-Auth attack**: The rogue client sends a high volume of “De-Auth” traffic, so clients are always de-auth.
    
*   **Dis-association attack**: The rogue client sends a high volume of “**Dis-association**” traffic, so clients are always disassociated.
    
*   **Attacked Party**: Either specific client (MAC address) or broadcast (all MAC ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff)
    
*   **More Details**: [https://docs.engenius.ai/whitepapers/airguard/malicious-attacks](https://docs.engenius.ai/whitepapers/airguard/malicious-attacks)
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252Fu7QrZEZqGpgcs9NKIvJw%252F1649915603935.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f2390e0-c050-4e35-b599-30f2213c3368&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=604bf816&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/airguard#rf-jamming)

RF Jamming


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

RF Jammer sends RF noise on a certain channel to increase the SNR rate or keep the SSID/channel busy, so the client cannot connect to SSIDs on the channel.

**More details**: [https://docs.engenius.ai/whitepapers/airguard/rf-jamming](https://docs.engenius.ai/whitepapers/airguard/rf-jamming)

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FSqT6MYi5LAbJerT1WwNE%252F1649915780902.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44ef6c67-7349-4d5c-8b2d-99ac019b6c19&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b97d328c&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-access-point/airguard#other-ssid)

Other SSID


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   There are many BYOD devices (employee’s mobile phones) broadcasting SSID for their own use, which is harmless
    
*   Whitelisted SSID
    
*   **More Details** : [https://docs.engenius.ai/whitepapers/airguard/rules-and-classifications#other-ssids](https://docs.engenius.ai/whitepapers/airguard/rules-and-classifications#other-ssids)
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FMeW8jOtsiQJQ26aikbqG%252F1649916053787.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c9d5665-0ce8-4433-8e78-a3e3ad1a4cec&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=924583d1&sv=2)

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

# Diag Tools | Cloud User Manual

This allows you to run the diagnostic tests that can help the Network administrator to troubleshoot.

Under switch detail page > you can easily see the “Diag Tools” icon

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FQRYAXsuWjZFHWKtB6v6s%252F1649405253567.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da3b8ef82-75c3-42ff-ba59-917867187692&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bbfdea2b&sv=2)

Under Manage > Switches > Diag

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FOzLgUfX2OXTtm4coAEvj%252F%25E8%259E%25A2%25E5%25B9%2595%25E5%25BF%25AB%25E7%2585%25A7%25202022-04-11%252013.25.06.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7fd74960-faf4-47ca-82fe-610187e54ff5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3af7d393&sv=2)

So the Full-screen tools are displayed, So you can use them.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F9aeiiGGUAfT67CUa0Ksr%252F1649654832597.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee58b6d6-c5c9-43ab-bd10-12e731bbc476&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=79411b8d&sv=2)

The Switch diag tool is required SW firmware V1.2.60 and above except for Packet capture is V1.2.61 and above.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diag-tools#activity)

Activity


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Overall port status view - It’s a good way to let users see all ports throughput at a glance

The bar indicates the throughput of the port and the color of the bar indicates the speed of the port.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F1XDS5UGe7b6QC5YBYtde%252F1649663128113.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99b65ae7-9a23-4c14-8949-0a6ff4b6d0b4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=33975176&sv=2)

CRC error

This is an important indication to see if anything is wrong with the transmission including the cable issues. The red square indicates there are CRC errors found. Users can mouse over to the port and see more details of throughput and CRC error count.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FQpWDUQRw4OjSeYSBZI1Q%252F1649663325506.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4cb3e770-8d45-4d25-bfb9-1242f0adff24&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b1357905&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diag-tools#clients-list-fdb)

Clients list (FDB)


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is the real-time client list of the Switch or the content of the forwarding table. Users can refresh the table by clicking the **refresh** button

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FNmXAOnEU12n0xrXErRD3%252F1649664314090.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D37a796e1-321b-44d3-9c93-bc871380ca57&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7a654a71&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diag-tools#cable-diag)

Cable Diag


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cable diag helps to check the Cable status of selected ports. (It can be multiple selections) and will show the possible distance of breaking points.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F1tUvNGWP3QXpEE3vZ3JJ%252F1649660692606.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc2ec4c74-07e5-43c6-a50e-6926ebad0210&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=840d58ee&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diag-tools#arp-table)

ARP Table


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In order to send packets on LAN, network devices need to know the IP and MAC address of the hosts they intend to communicate with. Address Resolution Protocol provides the mechanism to determine the MAC address associated with an IP address. These IP to MAC bindings are stored in each switch's ARP cache.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FAUCL8cPrYOVQnhHcKA1l%252F1649671460956.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D098392d3-b4a1-40ae-9103-36de2eb696be&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f008065&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diag-tools#packet-capture)

Packet Capture


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The packet capture utility can be used to observe live network traffic passed by EnGenius Switches. Since captures provide a live snapshot of traffic on the network, they can be immensely helpful in diagnosing and troubleshooting network issues. This article outlines how to remotely take a packet capture in Diag tools.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252Fwa9AsyssnwGlQGxSARhC%252F1649746345589.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D576e740d-7652-46ca-9e16-b1e6f188049e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=91be5162&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diag-tools#how-to-use-it)

How to use it

1.  Choose ports to capture packets > input Duration in sec > click on “Capture”, then the Switch will collect the packets and download them with the .pcap file
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FpNCo8IcMXWeMjKGu212q%252F1649747214356.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddfcd4642-f792-429c-879e-783a432ac7c0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e887ce90&sv=2)

2\. Download Wireshark or other packet analysis tools to open up the .pcap file

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FovkxaeQAfsiDEMGI82hi%252F1649747473477.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D841fba4d-ee21-4591-8f47-911c0cdfd2c3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f2510fb7&sv=2)

# PoE scheduling | Cloud User Manual

This allows you to view and configure PoE schedules that can be applied to the ports. Below screens display the existing schedules visually. Click **Manage > Switch lists > detail > PoE scheduling** to access this screen

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Select the ports to be set the PoE scheduling then click Edit
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-MUNMrFv9tE9KwyM3dg8%252F-MUNRuohcXziJGakZf7X%252F1614244169466.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da584b89d-3155-4e6d-8551-d7c4a0e7b1e3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a211842e&sv=2)

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-MUNS8k9p1qC9P4k0Zhe%252F-MUNSR-Y57th2xJR2dCp%252F1614244283995.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3601ac51-4dec-491a-a353-a6238bfde86a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fb8dcd97&sv=2)

4\. Click Apply.

# PD/Auto-Cam Lifeguard | Cloud User Manual

PDLG is a function that will automatically reboot PD devices when PoE switch found it was not responding. Which minimizes the downtime of network services and reduces admin effort via automatic processes.

*   In PDLG force ping mode, user have to set PD device IP manually. By keep pinging PDs, switch knows if PD is still alive or has to be rebooted.
    
*   PDLG also support auto mode which allows switch collecting PD information/status through LLDP preventing any PD IP changes under DHCP environment.
    
*   By fine tuning the reboot profiles, PDLG can correctly detects/reboot various PDs since every PD devices may have different response or bootup time.
    

ACLG is one of the option in PDLG auto mode. By enable ACLG, switch also considers Onvif discovery result to verify if the connected PD is surveillance device or not. Once switch make sure it is a surveillance device, it applies a ACLG reboot profile to corresponding port automatically.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F0rtPMaDkpkzjuv3oSTth%252F1701936014191.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd440fa27-cbe7-4b62-9ec4-44ad58775a6b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fbd9de8d&sv=2)

*   **Specified IP**: Setting specified IP on a specific port.
    
*   **Ping Interval:** Setting ping IP interval on a specific port.
    
*   **Ping Max Count**: Setting ping max count on a specific port.
    
*   **Power Recovery Interval:** The waiting time between power off and power on a specific port.
    
*   **PD BootUp Time:** Setting Powered Device boot-up time on a specific port.
    
*   **Reboot Max retry count** : Setting the max number of reboot
    
*   **LLDP/ACLG Expiry pending time:** Settings the corresponding LLDP expiry pending time.
    

The default value of PDLG ＆ ACLG is from the network wide profile settings

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FZ7MyDHa9CrhSG7q6MUN3%252F1701937977505.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a9981d2-f8af-4c00-bdc9-a11d06f6d8f0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=73dfa350&sv=2)

You can click lock icon to override the settings

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252F5TH4j7gd9B0DX6PWap4o%252F1701938316845.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c835644-25d1-406b-8f4f-a75625558d5c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72279018&sv=2)

**Must know**

ECS1xxx/2xxx - Switch firmware v1.2.80 or later

ECS5xxx - Switch firmware v2.2.10 or later

Last updated 1 year ago
