# Getting Switch Analytics | Cloud User Manual

From the **Switches** page, you can click **Details** on the web interface to display detailed information about a switch.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LmbshPNJz-UYK6CaFxV%252F-LmbsjGFaFxz_qiM29zh%252F1566184744820.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3afd1698-62c3-4259-9461-9e47944b3c42&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dae16da2&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diagnosing-a-switch#summary)

Summary


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**PoE reset from the Switch Panel :** User can mouse-over to the PoE port of the switch port panel and power-cycle the port, so the device attached to the port will be rebooted

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-MUNiYzEKfRRE_vWZZ4T%252F-MUNisb_551FUpBQZV51%252F1614248883944.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D171bee16-bcc0-4979-ae38-a4bcacfd6554&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d4b09c6c&sv=2)

**Total PoE Usage:** This bar graph displays the consumed, remaining, and total wattage utilized by Power over Ethernet.

**Total PoE Utilization by Port:** Displays the current PoE utilization by each port, in watts.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LmcLlpLglRk2kIqVp9U%252F-LmcLvnqlLzdvNSVCRMT%252F1566192609383.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0fb1038c-5eb0-4e05-82ab-0be58afce40f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=34da715a&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diagnosing-a-switch#system-setting)

System Setting


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The System Settings section allows you to configure all primary networking options for your switch.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diagnosing-a-switch#spanning-tree-protocol)

**Spanning Tree Protocol**

A **Spanning Tree Protocol** is a Layer 2 protocol that prevents loops in a network with redundant paths created by multiple switches. We recommend using this feature if your environment incorporates multiple switches.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LmcMzh3EX2F8kXYl228%252F-LmcN5dhDvzl1X4y2Pmz%252F1566192931347.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddfdfac28-b73d-4b51-bc73-9f7def048237&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bc23d397&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diagnosing-a-switch#procedure)

Procedure

1.  **Enable** the **STP** option
    
2.  Select a **Protocol**
    
3.  Select a **Bridge Priority** value
    
4.  Click **Apply**
    

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diagnosing-a-switch#lldp)

LLDP

The **Link Layer Discovery Protocol (LLDP)** is a Layer 2, vendor-neutral protocol that allows network devices to advertise capabilities, identity, and other information. This data can potentially be queried by SNMP.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LmcNdH0qfVq_TxJ4gZl%252F-LmcNfs6811OJdq4suKH%252F1566193105968.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba51a3cb-c2bd-4fd2-9b49-dd42e9ee0cf2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ead51303&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diagnosing-a-switch#procedure-1)

Procedure

1.  **Enable** the **LLDP** option
    
2.  Click **Apply**
    

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diagnosing-a-switch#voice-vlan)

Voice VLAN

The **Voice VLAN** feature configures switches to automatically allow and prioritize voice traffic over a designated VLAN. This keeps voice traffic separate and prioritized over other traffic types.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LmcOO9i0ls-onP1FM3X%252F-LmcOS4-tz6IZg6dUoS0%252F1566193286852.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D191ddac4-5d70-42af-80b0-2b9c7055cfbe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d4d8ed2&sv=2)

**Mode:** Allows you to define the Voice VLAN mode.

*   **Auto**: Automatically advertises the Voice VLAN to connected devices via the LLDP-MED protocol.
    
*   **OUIs**: Determines whether a received packet is a voice packet by checking its source MAC address.
    

**Switch Voice VLAN**: Allows you to choose what VLAN is used for Voice VLAN. You can set up VLANs in Port Settings.

**QoS Priority:** Lets you define whether the switch will use the Quality of Service CoS value of the incoming packet, or tag the packet with a CoS value between 1-7.

**OUIs:** VoIP traffic has a pre-configured Organizationally Unique Identifier (OUI) prefix in the source MAC address. You can manually add a specific manufacturer's MAC address and description to the OUI table. All traffic received on the Voice VLAN ports from the specific IP phone with a listed OUI is forwarded on the voice VLAN.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diagnosing-a-switch#qos)

**QoS**

Quality of service (QoS) allows operators to prioritize application traffic to ensure that latency-affected data, such as VoIP and video conferencing, is uninterrupted during periods of network congestion. Switches implement this by reading tagged packets and prioritizing them accordingly. Packets are classified using **Class of Service (CoS)** on the data link layer, and **Differentiated Services Code Points (DSCP)** on the network layer, mapped to a queue, then sent out accordingly as per QoS.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LmcOlZaTcBJsGa824Wo%252F-LmcOpfzEYzDDz52PCKB%252F1566193415352.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5076c998-5692-4eaf-9e24-dd97073064e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c6be4b65&sv=2)

**Trust Mode:** Allows you to define whether the switch will use CoS, DSCP, or both trust modes for QoS.

**Scheduling Method:** Allows you to define what method the switch will use when assessing transmitting incoming packets in queues. **Strict priority** always prioritizes queues with a higher priority, while **Weighted Round Robin (WRR)** weights each queue by priority, then applies a round-robin policy when choosing packets for transmission. The queues are weighted as follows:

Queue

Weight

1

1

2

2

3

4

4

8

5

16

6

32

7

64

8

128

**Queue Mapping:** Tagged packets are sent to queues defined in this setting. For each CoS or DSCP value, you can choose the queue to which tagged packets are mapped.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diagnosing-a-switch#igmp)

IGMP

**IGMP Snooping** is used for controlling multicast traffic. It listens to IGMP messages being processed by the switch and prevents these messages from being sent to hosts not part of the respective multicast.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LmccDB8NOYZGODM5czI%252F-LmccImJyJzRT7ByUvwQ%252F1566197127602.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d146744-0e4c-4d72-8823-386c74b5f9c2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=43a23ebe&sv=2)

**Version:** The available IGMP Snooping versions are v2 and v3. You can select either/or in the **Version** dropdown.

**VLANS:** You can enable IGMP Snooping for any VLAN by selecting the corresponding checkbox next to the VLAN ID.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diagnosing-a-switch#jumbo-frame)

Jumbo Frame

Ethernet has used the 1500 byte frame size since its inception. Jumbo frames are network layer PDUs that have a size much larger than the typical 1500 byte Ethernet Maximum Transmission Unit (MTU) size. Jumbo frames extend Ethernet to 9000 bytes, making them large enough to carry an 8 KB application datagram plus packet header overhead. If you intend to leave the local area network at high speeds, the dynamics of TCP will require you to use large frame sizes.

The switch supports a jumbo frame size of up to **9216 bytes**. Jumbo frames need to be configured to work on the ingress and egress port of each device along the end-to-end transmission path. Furthermore, all devices in the network must also be consistent on the maximum jumbo frame size, so it is important to do a thorough investigation of all your devices in the communication paths to validate their settings.

**Jumbo Frame** : Enter the size of a jumbo frame. The range is from **1522 to 9216** bytes.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-Lmch4uV6spEejKAEezm%252F-LmchBC_UyImaEiEYBcM%252F1566198442147.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De700e54b-11c8-4f28-90e3-7ae97dd5e58f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=63468d17&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diagnosing-a-switch#port-settings)

Port Settings


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Selecting one or more ports and clicking **Configure** will display the following settings:

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FHEZDR0jNTsOGYRL6EqbD%252F1702452766023.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D098545c3-c3f2-446a-a4df-00785259dfb2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eac73ceb&sv=2)

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FWzfBjzGDkpbgoaSyai7h%252F1702452924213.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57ef0c35-6229-45ff-bdad-88a0732e7961&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c2d075b1&sv=2)

**Enabled:** Allows you to enable or disable the connection for this port.

**Label:** Allows you to add a descriptor for this port.

**Speed/Duplex:** Allows you to define the following speed/duplex communication settings for this port:

*   Auto**:** Speed/Duplex will auto-negotiate based on the connected node.
    
*   1Gbps / Full Duplex
    
*   100 Mbps / Full Duplex
    
*   100 Mbps / Half Duplex
    
*   10 Mbps / Full Duplex
    
*   10 Mbps / Half Duplex
    

**Power over Ethernet (PoE):** Allows you to power a connected device through an Ethernet cable using your switch.

**VLANs:** Allows you to group devices to create a partitioned network on the same LAN.

**Forward Ports**: By configuring the forward ports, ports can be separated into different groups where traffic between different group are blocked.

**Must know**

ECS1xxx/2xxx - Firmware v1.2.74 or later

ECS5xxx - Firware v2.2.3 or later

EXT – Firmware v1.0.10 or later

**Rate Limit**: Allows you to limit the amount of incoming and outgoing traffic in Mbps.

**Flow Control:** Enabling this will have the switch regulate traffic during times of congestion.

**QoS:** If QoS is enabled in **Switch Settings**, you can configure additional settings per port.

*   **CoS Value:** All incoming packets that lack a CoS value will use the one set in this dropdown.
    
*   **Trust CoS:** If checked, the switch will queue packets tagged with CoS into their designated queues. If unchecked, all packets will leave the same queue.
    

**VLAN Trunking**: This allows the specific ports to receive/forward VLAN without adding this port to the member port of a specific VLAN. please notice that VLAN trunking will override the current VLAN port member setting except management VLAN.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/diagnosing-a-switch#override-system-setting-on-the-switch-network-wide-setting)

Override System setting on the Switch Network-wide setting


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

System setting is followed by Switch setting from the **Configure** > **Switch settings** as default settings. If you want individual AP System settings to be different from the Switch Network- wide setting , you can click below part in the screen to override the setting .

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-LoJy_0_9H_eyBPF6OeA%252F-LoK-Wc0X6-o6CdV8x8_%252F1568015463875.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc9f3a7a3-c367-4be7-ad00-03a4ed198a2c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=77a74d54&sv=2)

# License Expiration | EnGenius Cloud Licensing

The validity period of the license for each device managed by EnGenius Cloud is independent. If the license of one device has expired, it will not impact other devices with valid licenses. You can still use the professional features and manage these devices whose licenses are still valid.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3299519939-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MWghGkmPM86t8ANp9kZ%252Fuploads%252FOq8PXWS5gDFh5fFYWtVG%252FExpired%2520Device.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D229fc655-c183-43b6-8113-41535467e34b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f6e812fc&sv=2)

Diagram 4 - License expiration for devices

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-overview/license-expiration#when-the-license-of-a-device-in-the-managed-network-expires)

**When the license of a device in the managed Network expires:**

*   When one of the devices exceeds the expired date of its license, the license-expired device is still functional as usual, but cannot be managed(off-lined) by EnGenius Cloud or using any Cloud-related features like Cloud authentication. _(Device D license is expired and off-lined)_
    
*   The other devices within the same Network with a valid license won’t be affected by the use of professional features. _(Device A&B will still be managed even Device D license is expired)_
    
*   If the Feature Plan is changed **from PRO to Basic**, all your devices (expired or active) can then be managed by EnGenius Cloud, all privileges exceed Basic limit will be erased and Pro features will be disabled. (see [Feature Plans Comparison](https://www.engenius.ai/cloud/licenses)
    )
    

For a license-expired device, to manage it with EnGenius Cloud again:

1.  Add a new license to the device (with professional features)
    
2.  Change the Feature Plan from PRO to Basic. (without professional features)
    

Last updated 1 year ago

---

# License Status & Lifecycle | EnGenius Cloud Licensing

The following diagram reveals the various statuses and operations performed on a license.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3299519939-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MkFTP6mPDb3kJRwf2Rb%252Fuploads%252FLgws2P3EGNMIYlu1wqKQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D64181302-94cf-4f54-b52a-63e9b7444c5e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=77012a39&sv=2)

Terms

Description

**License Key Issue Date**

The date when a license key is issued and mailed

**Activation Date**

The date a licensed-associated device is assigned to a managed network.

**Forced-activtion Date**

The date that the license is auto-activated because of no activation on any device after 90 days of being issued.

**Expiration Date**

One year or three years after the license activation date. For a licensed device, the expired date means extending the validation of its original expired date

**Order Return**

The license order can be returned within one month after the license key is issued. (This is subject to the operation of each region. Please contact your local EnGenius)

**Undo License Association**

You can disassociate the license from a device within seven days after it's associated.

Last updated 1 year ago

# Mirror | Cloud User Manual

Port Mirroring allows you to copy packets on one or more ports to a mirroring destination port. You can attach a monitoring device to the mirroring destination port to view details about the packets passing through the copied ports. This is useful for network monitoring and troubleshooting purposes. The feature is available is at **Manage** > **Switch** < **Details** > **Mirror**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-M5Zx9OD3TIgOFNyxtho%252F-M5_3lQs9gpzmKnay253%252F1587612386801.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D60a116d8-611d-4194-aecf-b2cfd90d2031&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=33ba7d37&sv=2)

The following describe the labels on this screen :

**Session id** : A number identifying the mirror session. Switch supports up to 3 mirror sessions.

**Session State** : Select whether to enable or disable port mirroring.

**Destination Port :** The port which all mirrored data is sent to **.**

**Ingress** : indicates that only data being received will be mirrored.

**Egress** : indicates that only data being sent will be mirrored

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/mirror#how-to-configure)

How to configure


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Click the edit icon towards the right .
    
2.  Enable the **Session state.**
    
3.  Select the **Destination port**
    
4.  Select the **Ingress** and **Egress** port
    
5.  Click **Apply**
    

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/mirror#port-state)

Port state


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are four types of port that you configured .

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-M5tRLFIlQ9F1ytNlhte%252F-M5tUdv7G1B-5j875i-5%252F1587954837584.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7dc9874d-041f-49e5-9a68-007a9f5389fd&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=68362c02&sv=2) Port was assigned to a destination port . ![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-M5tRLFIlQ9F1ytNlhte%252F-M5tV0z1jdrsSIobKTbv%252F1587954846277.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd2fc0b21-5df2-44a0-9862-01d5fd4220e3&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=47c0d181&sv=2) Port was assigned only data being sent will be mirrored . ![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-M5tRLFIlQ9F1ytNlhte%252F-M5tVVUAciCbl6iomCMV%252F1587954857565.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dffb4027e-ccd7-4c0c-b1cf-ca98728021db&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2c6c1c40&sv=2) Port was assigned only data being received will be mirrored . ![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-M5tRLFIlQ9F1ytNlhte%252F-M5tVZtLqIoYkKYAwIB2%252F1587954920670.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9519235a-fdbb-4cc0-be0e-4b8829c99b4c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a9a6440&sv=2) Port was assigned both directions of data are being mirrored to the destination port.

# VLANs | Cloud User Manual

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/switch-setting#manually-configuring-vlans-individually)

Manually Configuring VLANs individually


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

you can access this page through **Configure** > **Switches** > **Detail** > **VLAN**

Using the **VLAN** tab, you can manually configure VLANs on the switch. Click **Add** to add another VLAN.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FDw5VmnIzoWUiY6AKWsTb%252F1670562470349.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1921705d-db9a-44e6-9eca-a8587ce39b84&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3f8ea43a&sv=2)

enter the VLAN ID and VLAN name of the switch.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FbeOqMb9zmhFibz1DK9Qu%252F1670562538070.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D33b0d61f-4dbf-4e35-b8c1-4c2cd2dcccc3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=89fe44a3&sv=2)

Click the edit button to have the Port Assignment.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FynhMAqvxHfMzsrFX5lMe%252F1670562976300.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6d509229-5b78-4af8-8b08-9b182b687b02&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2e855f0a&sv=2)

You can click the Tagged field or Untagged field to assign the tagged / Untagged port.

The (T) indicates the ports that will have Tagged data.

The (U) indicates the ports that will have data Untagged

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FsNW4rw1YK5NBMlo1jNon%252F1670563100582.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb14bf84-5cb6-4a92-af79-90a1d40a7019&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6bfb21a0&sv=2)

If you used to input manually. You can click the pencil icon to input the port numbers.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FenAXuXnjDkctUYDutAwS%252F1670563561470.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56fd6361-91eb-4e07-8b3a-b4b9796e503b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2d59ea9e&sv=2)

Remember to click **Apply** to finalize the settings

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FmH375peDxrkA4Ds4c4GK%252F1670563655998.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94b78643-0c46-4725-90ab-9a3840be5171&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d71e8fb3&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/switch-setting#configure-multiple-vlans-at-a-time-using-a-json-file)

Configure multiple VLANs at a time using a JSON file


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For Apartments or other network environments, a network administrator might need to create VLANs for each unit, so needs to create hundreds of VLANs for the whole network switches. This will help the network admin to configure VLAN at a time instead of creating the VLAN one by one in each switch.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/switch-setting#vlan-export)

VLAN Export

This will export the current VLAN JSON file of the switch and allows you to edit locally.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FXYyM0mFdYbgPkfo8yFjd%252F1670564007927.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddc0b89a1-3f26-412b-b848-7d25ba40b7af&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7ee30dc&sv=2)

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/switch-setting#vlan-import)

VLAN Import


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can manually set up multiple VLANs for a specific switch by importing a JSON file.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FZ3MNixzl9DQii4uHZRNH%252F1670564131480.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47708a2c-c71d-4389-a190-2ed871d91d21&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2f8d0a1c&sv=2)

Click the **example** hyperlink to download the JSON file

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FWLhffZ4ZgOc8sjWv6X6V%252F1670554140046.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d012034-3562-4b62-ad8d-dc0a40f6b43f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=85ac7301&sv=2)

and then adjust the VLAN settings locally

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FxCdhSNsIYgJxt0v42r03%252F1670554229826.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0786acad-16e2-4611-b455-2401a734e471&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4921ff6f&sv=2)

then click **JSON file upload** to import your custom JSON file.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252Fuploads%252FaMchcfSUgjy90WbY6l2P%252F1670553415987.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9c6838b-5ff2-4aec-9b2c-b58f883f31ff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e47ab00b&sv=2)

So you can import VLAN settings at a time instead use the current Web GUI to edit them one by one. Please notice that It will override your VLAN settings if you ever create the VLAN manually.

After a single configuration, you can go to another Switch VLAN setting page to import the same text file, so to save time to go over the creation.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/switch-setting#undefined)

# LLDP-MED | Cloud White Papers

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/lldp-med#voice-vlan)

Voice VLAN


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Current ECS switches already support LLDP-MED to configure voice vlan of IP phones automatically. In "switch settings" page (also available in network-wide setting):

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2788256466-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Lo1AtG4HHv3uJq1FqqB%252F-MHzBvFY2gkNoOBuX77F%252F-MHzDSDj3xw08Xt-qDWi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D73311622-88f0-44c8-872d-cad9cd791e7d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=838bb7dc&sv=2)

set voice vlan mode to "auto" will make the switch continuously send voice vlan and its priority TLVs via LLDP-MED. The IP phone would adopt that VLAN and priority if it supports the same standard.

# Add License | EnGenius Cloud Licensing

To enable professional features for managed devices, you need to purchase **PRO License Key** from EnGenius resellers first and add it to your managed **Organization**.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-overview/add-license#adding-a-license-to-the-organization)

**Adding a license to the Organization**

1.  Login to EnGenius Cloud and select the managed Organization
    
2.  Go to _**Inventory & License > Licenses**_
    
3.  Click ' **\+ Add License**' on the right
    
4.  Enter the **purchased license key(s)** and the system will unzip the license key(s) into one or multiple licenses. Click "OK", adding to Organization
    
5.  All licenses added will be displayed in the license table with related license information.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3299519939-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MkFTP6mPDb3kJRwf2Rb%252Fuploads%252FXKzsgZKcaAeORNEE3wB6%252Fadd%2520license.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9acfbb8c-8570-4de5-bd2a-4fb9bd8af99c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8a7c1820&sv=2)

Figure 1 - Assign license to organization

Last updated 1 year ago

---

# Associate License | EnGenius Cloud Licensing

Associate a license means to bundle a license to a specific device.

After you select PRO Feature Plan and already added license to the Organization, you need to associate license(s) to the device(s) and assign the device(s) into a managed Network, thus those devices can use Professional features.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-overview/associate-license#associate-license-s-with-the-device-s)

**Associate license(s) with the device(s)**

1.  Login to EnGenius Cloud and select the managed Organization
    
2.  Go to _**Inventory & License > Devices**_
    
3.  Click ' **\+ Assign License**' at the right of each device
    
4.  Select any available and valid license(s) to associate it to the device
    
5.  License-associated device(s) will display the information for license status and the expiration date.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3299519939-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MkFTP6mPDb3kJRwf2Rb%252Fuploads%252FjOqS1uP7p8kjVwb5HEFb%252Fnew%2520device.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8e7d420-bd32-4fb3-94f5-7378aa09ba4d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9a8ef8f&sv=2)

Figure 2 - Assign license(s) to a device

If more than two licenses are installed on the same device within a 7-day grace period, only one license can be disassociated, and the remaining licenses cannot be disassociated.

Last updated 1 year ago

---

# Presence Service | Cloud White Papers

For applications like CRM tools, presence analytics, or location-aware services which need to continuously gather presence data of wireless clients, EnGenius Cloud Acess Points are capable of delivering realtime presence data to fulfill the requirement.

EnGenius Presence Service can have cloud managed APs continuously gathering 802.11 probe request frames sent by wireless clients and then sending the data to 3rd party servers configured in EnGenius Cloud.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/presence-service#configuration)

Configuration


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In EnGeniusCloud, the configuration of presence service is at

> **General Settings** > **AP** > **Advanced Settings**

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2788256466-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Lo1AtG4HHv3uJq1FqqB%252F-Lz-nLWUzIONTLQeo1YL%252F-Lz0-mvEjmszWsKt94KD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70e4b9bc-32be-42e9-8dfb-1aeba83e4404&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=67c45427&sv=2)

Following parameters can be configured in the page:

Parameters

Description

Server Location

3rd party server address

Key

Secret used to generate a SHA256 HMAC signature, over the payload (the JSON message). The signature is then added to a custom HTTP header (“Signature”) in the POST message.

Interval

Interval between two consecutive message been sent.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/presence-service#data-format)

Data Format


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The data sent by EnGenius Presence Services is basically in JSON format with following objects:

Object

Description

mac

MAC address of the **end client device** for which presence data is being reported.

node\_mac

MAC address of the **Access Point** reporting the presence data.

min\_signal

Lowest RSSI reading on the access point for the specific client within the time period specified by the **First seen** and **Last seen** timestamps.

max\_signal

Highest RSSI reading on the AP for the specific client within the time period specified by the **First seen** and **Last seen** timestamps.

count

Number of times the specific end client device connected to the access point within the time period specified by the **First seen** and **Last seen** timestamps.

avg\_signal

Average RSSI reading on the AP for the specific client within the time period specified by the **First seen** and **Last seen** timestamps.

first\_seen

Timestamp of when the client was first seen, during the reporting period; timezone is UTC.

last\_seen

Timestamp of when the client was last seen, during the reporting period; timezone is UTC.

last\_seen\_signal

Reported RSSI reading on the access point for when this client was last seen.

associated

Displays the association status between the client and the access point.

The server receives the data via an HTTP POST message. Access points and EnGenius Cloud services DO NOT keep any of presence data. Accordingly, if the server specified in the configuration is down or otherwise unreachable, the HTTP POST will fail, making the data inaccessible. EnGenius Cloud will not provide any notification of such failure.

Last updated 3 years ago

Was this helpful?

# Link Aggregation | Cloud User Manual

Link aggregation groups multiple ports together in parallel to act as a single logical link. Aggregation-enabled devices treat all physical links (ports) in an aggregation group entirely as a single logical link (port). Member ports in an aggregation group share egress/ingress traffic load, delivering a bandwidth that is multiple of a single physical link. The feature is available is at **Manage** > **Switch** < **Details** > **Link Aggregation**

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/managing-devices/managing-switches/link-aggregation#how-to-configure)

**How to Configure**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To Configure trunk , you must select **aggregation type** . Select from the following options:

*   **LACP**: LACP is a dynamic protocol which helps to automate the configuration and maintenance of LAG’s. The main purpose of LACP is to automatically configure individual links to an aggregate bundle, while adding new links and helping to recover from link failures if the need arises. LACP can monitor to verify if all the links are connected to the authorized group. LACP is a standard in computer networking, hence LACP should be enabled on the Switch's trunk ports initially in order for both the participating Switches/devices that support the standard to use it.
    
*   **Static:** Static configuration is used when connecting to a switch that doesn't support LACP.
    
*   **Disable** : Disable the trunk that you configured previously.
    

Then select the **Member Ports** to add into the trunk group. There are two ways to select the ports

1.  Click on the port picker to select multiple ports.
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-M5_rJsuxfzdj7Rm2M62%252F-M5_tQqpzA9GaO2uy8R8%252F1587626122184.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd01c626-9fe9-4ef2-b931-5b7ec1e122f7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eadfcff2&sv=2)

2\. Click Pencil icon to input port numbers

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-M5aQBEv2VagA1wwXxpd%252F-M5aU-f8oadXuD328sg7%252F1587635792891.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d041992-5a8f-4b4d-a7b9-723498ddbbcd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=48d380f8&sv=2)

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-M5aQBEv2VagA1wwXxpd%252F-M5aU9DUv7rh4B0Vet8z%252F1587635768479.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0f131391-df08-46e4-a0e7-aed5fb495b5d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=649afe38&sv=2)

After you complete the trunk settings , remember to click **Apply** to take effect .

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3893603398-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LgVsoqihVR3I0VRYmyO%252F-M5e-a0NFlUt9Ne2BEag%252F-M5e0JxBaLyqXtLqx_Qx%252F1587695366490.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc419e98c-1839-416f-831e-6f3b5e33b9db&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3f5e441f&sv=2)

# Move License | EnGenius Cloud Licensing

EnGenius Cloud licensing allows administrators to move the licenses and devices between Organizations in the following use cases.

*   Move device(s) and transfer associated licenses to another Organization
    
*   Move unassociated licenses to another Organization directly
    

When you move around licenses and devices between Organizations, you need to have privileges (**Organization administrator**) on both sides.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-overview/move-license#moving-unassociated-licenses)

Moving unassociated licenses

*   Only the unassociated license, the license with the empty association, can be moved to another **Organization**
    

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-overview/move-license#moving-device-s-with-licenses)

Moving device(s) with licenses

*   When the device is moved to another **Organization**, the associated licenses will be moved simultaneously.
    
*   The license information will remain the same whenever you move devices (associated licenses) to another Organization.
    
    *   License Issue date
        
    *   License Activation date
        
    *   License Status
        
    

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3299519939-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MkFTP6mPDb3kJRwf2Rb%252Fuploads%252FWXzqy1VTGGCaAu0I9t0b%252FMove%2520device%2520nad%2520license.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def4a306f-ae1f-4285-865d-b1bb21ed3f7e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9f0ad1e0&sv=2)

Move device B with licenses between Organization (From Organization A to Organization B)

# Captive Portal | Cloud White Papers

A captive portal presents a web page (also known as a ‘“splash page”) which requires action on the part of the user before network access is granted. The required action can be simply viewing and agreeing to an acceptable use policy, or entering a user ID and password which must be validated against a database of authorized users.

When a captive portal is enabled, all Internet traffic will be re-directed to a particular URL and a user is required to take specific actions before their traffic is able to pass through to the Internet. In this way, a service provider controls the initial Internet experience for their end customer can request the customer take a variety of actions:

1.  accept a set of terms and conditions before being allowed onto the Internet.
    
2.  fill out a survey.
    
3.  purchase a billing plan
    
4.  view an advertisement
    

EnGeniusCloud includes built-in captive portal functionality with features like pre-built templates for free click-through access and powerful external captive portal APIs, which can allow customers and partners to deploy and leverage their own captive portal and billing systems, enabling a limitless range of applications such as specialized coupons and user analytics.

In order for the Captive Portal to function the EnGeniusCloud must be reachable at all times. Guests are redirected to the EnGeniusCloud to reach the guest portal, and the redirection will not be successful if Cloud APIs is not accessible.

Last updated 5 years ago

Was this helpful?

---

# Integrate with External Splash Page | Cloud White Papers

Using an external splash page allows you full control over the sequencing and presentation of a splash page. Alternatively, [i](https://help.cloudtrax.com/hc/en-us/articles/204803954-Internally-Hosted-Splash-Page-with-RADIUS-Authentication)
nternal splash page are simpler, but provide less flexibility. External splash pages are stored and executed on a web server that user define, and must respond appropriately to certain messages from the Access Point in order to present appropriate user-interface to the user at various stages of the authentication process.

When combined with RADIUS Authentication, EnGeniusCloud will consult an external RADIUS server that you specify in order to determine whether to authenticate the user. The user interface presented to the user will be determined by the external splash page.

Most EnGenius customers who need a captive portal authentication system on their wireless networks use the customizable splash pages that are hosted by EnGeniusCloud. However, some network administrators may prefer to host a captive portal page on their own servers. This Section shows you how to configure EnGeniusCloud to adopt external splash page with an external RADIUS server to handle authentication.

Last updated 5 years ago

Was this helpful?

# General Licensing | EnGenius Cloud Licensing

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/general-licensing#can-i-keep-using-the-basic-plan-for-free)

Can I keep using the Basic plan for free?

> YES. The Basic plan feature set includes the most-frequent-used features already and is perfectly suitable for SMB. If you don't need the advanced features, you can keep using the Basic features as before without any license required.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/general-licensing#how-do-i-change-my-feature-plan-in-the-org)

How do I change my feature plan in the Org?

> User can switch between Basic and Pro plan anytime manually under _**Org > Inventory & License.**_ However, please be reminded that if you want to use the Pro plan, make sure you have the Pro license associated with the devices you wish to manage.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/general-licensing#can-i-have-different-plans-for-different-networks)

Can I have different plans for different Networks?

> The Feature Plan is per Org basis and applies to all Networks under the Org. With the hierachical view design, users should be very easy to manage multiple Orgs with different feature plans under a single-pane-of-glass.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/general-licensing#how-do-i-purchase-a-cloud-license-and-apply-to-a-device)

How do I purchase a Cloud license and apply to a device?

> 1.  Contact your local EnGenius Resellers or EnGenius for details
>     
> 2.  Place the license order (had better a separated license order from hardware order) with a mail list which you would like the license key to be mailed to
>     
> 3.  One License Key will be generated per each line of the License Order (i.e. AP-1YR-LIC \* 10)
>     
> 4.  People in the mail list will then receive a mail with multiple PDF files. Each PDF file includes one unique License Key. For example, for a license order with 2 lines, AP-1YR-LIC \* 10 and SW-1YR-LIC \* 5, you will receive 2 PDF files in the mail, one with License Key of AP-1YR-LIC \* 10 and the other one with License Key of SW-1YR-LIC \* 5
>     
> 5.  You then can enter the License Key in the _**Inventory & License > License > Add license**_, where you can double-check the content of the License Key before applying.
>     
> 6.  Once the License Key is applied, multiple licenses will be generated by the License Key in the License page. In this case, 10 lines of AP-1YR-LIC and 5 lines of SW-1YR-LIC will be generated on the license page
>     
> 7.  You then can associate each License to a device.
>     

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/general-licensing#how-many-types-of-cloud-licenses)

How many types of Cloud licenses?

> Cloud feature Plan includes Basic and Pro plan. For the "**Basic**" plan, no license is required for a device. However, for the "**PRO**" plan, users need to purchase a "**PRO**" license for each device.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/general-licensing#do-i-have-to-purchase-switch-pro-license-if-i-only-need-ap-pro-features)

Do I have to purchase Switch Pro license if I only need AP Pro features?

> If you only need AP Pro features, you just need to purchase Pro licenses for your AP device and keep the Switch Feature Plan to "Basic" without any Switch license required.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/general-licensing#how-does-licensing-vary-between-different-engenius-product-lines-e.g.-wireless-switches)

How does licensing vary between different EnGenius product lines, e.g., wireless, switches?

> EnGenius offers the flexibility to choose your plan for different product types, i.e., users can set the AP feature plan to "**PRO**" while SW feature plan to "**Basic**" in the case that users only need to use "**PRO**" features in AP and no need for PRO features in SW.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/general-licensing#do-i-have-to-buy-more-licenses-every-time-i-buy-new-hardware)

Do I have to buy more licenses every time I buy new hardware?

> When a new device is purchased, the device comes with one year free **PRO** license starting from the date the user registers the device to an Organization.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/general-licensing#do-i-need-to-have-a-license-for-every-engenius-cloud-hardware)

Do I need to have a license for every EnGenius Cloud hardware?

> For the "**Basic**" feature plan, no license is required for devices. However, if the user chooses the "**PRO**" feature plan, then all devices of the category need to have a valid license (not expired) associated with the device to be able to be managed by Cloud.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/general-licensing#will-a-device-in-inventory-require-a-license)

Will a device in inventory require a license?

> No. Only when the device is assigned to a Network under the "**PRO**" feature plan requires a valid license. Other devices in inventory do not need any license.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/general-licensing#when-will-the-license-start-to-burn-count-down)

When will the license start to burn (count-down)?

> No. Only when the device is assigned to a Network under the "**PRO**" feature plan requires a valid license. Other devices in inventory do not need any license.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/general-licensing#will-the-device-still-be-functional-when-the-license-expires)

Will the device still be functional when the license expires?

> YES. If the license is expired under the "**PRO**" feature plan, the device can still be functional as before the license expired, but it can not be configurable nor manageable from the EnGenius Cloud platform.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/general-licensing#if-i-choose-the-basic-feature-plan-will-the-license-keep-burning)

If I choose the "Basic" feature plan, will the license keep burning?

> YES. When the license starts to burn from "activation date", it will keep burning (countdown) until "Expired date" no matter if the user chooses which feature plans (Basic or RRO).

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/general-licensing#any-free-trial-for-the-professional-feature-plan)

Any free trial for the professional feature plan?

> Every device comes with a 90-day free "**Pro**" license for users to try on the "**Pro**" features, starting from the date the user registers the device to an Organization.

Last updated 3 months ago

---

# License Operation | EnGenius Cloud Licensing

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/license-operation#how-do-i-associate-the-license-with-the-device)

How do I associate the license with the device?

> A license can only be associated with a device; however, a device can have multiple licenses.
> 
> Two ways to add licenses:
> 
> 1.  Go to **Inventory & license > Devices page,** choose the device and click "Assign license".
>     
> 2.  Go to **Inventory & License > License page,** choose one available license, and associate to a device
>     

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/license-operation#what-happens-when-i-change-feature-plans-from-pro-to-basic)

What happens when I change feature plans from PRO to Basic?

> After changing the feature plan from PRO to Basic, those professional features won't be available anymore. The logs or users exceeding the limit of "**Basic**" plan will be deleted, and it cannot be undone, even user switches back from "Basic" to "PRO".

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/license-operation#what-happens-if-the-licensed-device-is-dis-registered-from-an-org)

What happens if the licensed device is dis-registered from an Org?

> When the device is dis-registered from an Organization, the licenses associated with the device will be gone, except the one-year free license that came with the newly purchased device.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/license-operation#will-the-90-day-free-trial-license-be-gone-when-the-device-is-unregistered-from-the-org)

Will the 90-day free trial license be gone when the device is unregistered from the Org?

> No. When the device is registered, the EnGenius Cloud will record the expired date (90 days after the registered date), so no matter how many times the device registers/un-register to a different Organization, the expired date of the free license will be kept the same.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/license-operation#can-i-move-licenses-between-organizations)

Can I move licenses between Organizations?

> Yes. You can move un-associated licenses to the other Organization you have the administrator privilege.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/license-operation#what-happens-if-i-move-a-device-with-multiple-licenses-to-another-organization)

What happens if I move a device with multiple licenses to another Organization?

> If the device has multiple licenses associated with it, all licenses will be moved to another Organization together with the device.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/license-operation#can-i-extract-a-license-from-an-organization)

Can I extract a license from an Organization?

> Users can move the license among the Organization the user has privilege. However, users cannot extract the license to re-enter other Organizations.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/license-operation#can-i-co-terminate-different-license-expiration-dates-for-devices)

Can I co-terminate different license expiration dates for devices?

> Yes. Users can purchase a **Co-Termination License** to add to the devices of a Network to make their expired date to be terminated on the same date. The **Co-Term Calculator** tool can help users to calculate how many units of Co-Termination license needs to be purchased.
> 
> For example, under same organization, there might be different networks with different accounting periods, so the termination date might be different. A **Co-Termination License** can ensure that the devices within a network have the same termination date.
> 
> It can be applied to multiple networks, but only to devices with 'Valid-License.

Last updated 12 days ago

---

# License Status | EnGenius Cloud Licensing

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/license-status#will-i-be-notified-before-my-license-expires)

Will I be notified before my license expires?

> By default, the system will automatically notify the user 60/30/3 days before any license is going to expire.

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/license-status#what-happens-when-the-devices-license-expires)

What happens when the device's license expires?

> If the feature plan is "**PRO**", then when the device's license is expired, Those devices with license expired will still be functional as usual, but cannot be managed nor change any configuration via the EnGenius Cloud platform until the user switches the Feature Plan from "Pro" to "Basic".

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud-licensing/license-guidelines/license-status#what-is-the-license-merging-merged-status)

What is the license merging/merged status?

> When a license is added to a device, there is a 7 days grace period to allow users to "undo" the association. Within the grace period, the license status is **Merging**. (Go to **Inventory & License > Licenses**)
> 
> After the grace period, the license will be bound with the device and cannot be unbundled. And then, the license status will change to **Merged**. (Go to **Inventory & License > Licenses**)
> 
> If more than two licenses are installed on the same device within a 7-day grace period, only one license can be disassociated, and the remaining licenses cannot be disassociated.

Last updated 12 days ago

---

# Click-through | Cloud White Papers

When captive portal is enabled and authentication type is set to "Click-through", the user is redirected to a splash page and clicks on a link to be granted access to the Internet.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/captive-portal/external-splash-page/click-through#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/captive-portal/external-splash-page/click-through#communication-flow)

Communication Flow

Following figure shows the communication flows and steps for a Click-through captive portal with external splash page server.

![](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2788256466-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Lo1AtG4HHv3uJq1FqqB%252F-LrEjugsnq6be4olJy7b%252F-LrEs5dGSVGdf0IZugHM%252Fexternal%2520splash%2520page.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd8c6039-679d-4543-b90c-7f2bca89eff3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=be9c104b&sv=2)

1.  A new wireless client tries to connect to a Captive Portal enabled SSID served by an Access Point.
    
2.  The AP intercepts the request and redirect the user to the external splash page which is served by a external web server configured in `SSID's splash page` setting. In addition, an `**actionurl**` parameter is passed to the splash page such that browser can be redirected back to the cloud after submission in splash page.
    
3.  Splash page content with `**actionurl**` parameter are delivered to browser.
    
4.  User clicks on the confirmation link or submit button in the splash page and then be redirected to `**actionurl**` to complete the authentication.
    

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/captive-portal/external-splash-page/click-through#parameters)

Parameters

In previous Section Step 2, the actionurl parameter is composed of a cloud URL with extra parameters. A https request sample to the splash page could be like this:

Copy

    https://yourwebsite.com/splash.html?actionurl=https://falcon.service.engenius.ai/captive-portal/auth%3Fuserurl=https://www.google.com/%26loginurl=http://192.168.200.1:4990/www/login.chi%26mac=0C:D2:92:42:0C:57%26called=8A:DC:96:21:FF:E5

The [https://yourwebsite.com/splash.html](https://xxxxx/splash.html)
 here is the splash page setting customized for corresponding SSID. The details of the actionurl parameters are listed as follows:

Parameter Name

Description

vendor

Should be "EnGenius"

ap\_ip

IP address of associated AP

ap\_mac

MAC address of associated AP

ap\_port

AP service port

client\_ip

IP address of the wireless client

client\_mac

MAC address of the wireless client

userurl

The URL that user tried to visit before authenticated

mac

Client's MAC address (will be obsolete after 2021)

please use **client\_mac**

called

AP's MAC address (will be obsolete after 2021)

please use **ap\_mac**

nas\_id

Network access server identifier is used to notify the source of a RADIUS access request.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/captive-portal/external-splash-page/click-through#enabling-an-external-splash-page-on-engeniuscloud)

Enabling an External Splash Page on EnGeniusCloud


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Select a network in [Org-tree](https://docs.engenius.ai/engenius-cloud/working-with-org-trees)
    .
    
2.  Select SSID in the configuring tool menu.
    
3.  Choose the SSID you want to configure.
    
4.  switch to `Captive Portal` Tab and make sure your Captive Portal is enabled and Authentication Type is set to "`Click-through`".
    
5.  switch to `Splash Page` Tab. Select "`External Splash Page URL"`.
    
6.  Enter the URL of your custom splash page (eg, https://yourwebsite.com/splash.html).
    
7.  Click on "`Apply`" button.
    

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/captive-portal/external-splash-page/click-through#configure-the-external-splash-page-server)

Configure the External Splash Page Server


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The external splash page must be hosted on a web server that will be accessible from the Access Points on your network. The following must be accomplished, but the particular details will depend very much on your web hosting environment.

1.  Setup the Web Server.
    
2.  Modify the splash page to set `**form action**` as the value of `**actionurl**` passed by cloud. In this way, after the user submit the form, he will be redirected to specific URL and complete the authentication.
    
3.  Another way to implement the splash page is to have a hyperlink redirect the browser to `actionurl`. For Example:
    
    `<a href="<?php print $_GET['actionurl'] ?>">For all in one url</a>`
    

Last updated 4 years ago

Was this helpful?

# Zero-wait DFS | Cloud White Papers

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/zero-wait-dfs#dfs)

DFS


--------------------------------------------------------------------------

Dynamic Frequency Selection (DFS) is a mandate for radio systems operating in the 5 GHz band to identify and avoid interference with Radar systems. IEEE 802.11h is the standard that covers the usage of DFS channels. To make use of DFS channels, wireless access points need to be certified to ensure that WiFi services on AP do follow the rule, e.g., stop immediately when a Radar signal is detected.

Since only a few business or enterprise APs are certified to use DFS channels, DFS channels are generally not so crowded in comparing with non-DFS channels. Network providers like to use DFS channels because of less interference. However, for the area with occasional Radar signals, service providers tend to avoid DFS channels.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/zero-wait-dfs#what-is-zero-wait-dfs)

What is Zero-wait DFS


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Based on the 802.11h standard, AP needs to change its channel immediately when the Radar signal is detected in the current DFS channel. In general, AP can only hop back to the non-DFS channel. The main reason is:

> According to 802.11h, an AP, when moving to a new DFS channel, has to listen silently to the medium for **one minute** before it is allowed to transmit anything (like a beacon) in order to make sure that no radar is currently operating on that channel.

AP cannot wait for one minute without serving its wireless clients. That's why falling back to regular non-DFS channels is the only way for conventional APs to comply with standards.

Instead of falling back to the non-DFS channel, zero-wait DFS is a technique providing the seamless change of channels. That is, stations do not lose their connectivity when an AP moves to another DFS channel. With the dedicated scanning radio, EnGenius S-series APs can always guarantee the one-minute clearance of the target DFS channel hence hop to that channel without any waiting.

When an AP changes its channel, Channel Switch Announcement (CSA), as defined by IEEE 802.11h, is adopted to announce that AP is switching to a new channel before it begins transmitting on that channel. This allows the clients, who support CSA, to transition to the new channel with minimal downtime.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/zero-wait-dfs#how-does-engenius-support-zero-wait-dfs)

How Does EnGenius Support Zero-wait DFS


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All S-series APs support zero-wait DFS. Relative options are available in radio settings.

Good to know:

*   Enable Spectrum Analyzer or Channel Scan in Live Diag would suspend zero-wait DFS temporarily because these Live Diag Tools need the scanning radio to scan all channels.
    
*   AirGuard may work with zero-wait DFS smoothly except the containment feature is enabled. The containment feature requires the scanning radio to do the containment in advance.
    

Last updated 5 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Error Message | Cloud White Papers

When a failed login occurs from Captive Portal, the user will be redirected to the splash page again with 2 additional query parameters **res** and **reason** to indicate the error. The https request to the splash page could be like this:

Copy

    https://yourwebsite.com/splash.html?actionurl=......&res=failed&reason=xxxx

These 2 parameters can be used for displaying error message on splash page. The usage is depicted in the following table:

Parameters

Description

res=failed&reason=reject

Invalid username or password.

res=failed&reason=timeout

No response from authentication server.

res=failed&reason=mtu

Abnormal network error.

res=failed&reason=other

Other errors.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/cloud-white-papers/captive-portal/external-splash-page/error-message#reference-code)

Reference Code


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following JavaScript code illustrates how to display error message in splash page.

Copy

       <script>
          function check_error(){
            const params = new Proxy(new URLSearchParams(window.location.search), {
              get: (searchParams, prop) => searchParams.get(prop),
            });
            if (params.res === "failed") {
              switch(params.reason) {
                case "reject":
                  alert("Invalid Username or Password.");
                  break;
                case "timeout":
                  alert("No response from authentication server.");
                  break;
                case "mtu":
                  alert("Abnormal network error.");
                  break;
                case "other":
                  alert("Other errors.");
                  break;
                default:
                  alert("Other errors. (no reason)");
              }
            }
          }
        </script>    
      </head>
    
      <body onload="check_error()" style="">

Was this helpful?

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/release-note/access-point-firmware/ecw536#appendix-for-v1.x.81)

**Appendix for v1.x.81**

1.  **Add support for SAMLv2 in Captive portal with Azure-AD**
    

A captive portal is a web page that users must interact with to gain network access, often seen in public Wi-Fi networks. This update introduces support for SAMLv2 (Security Assertion Markup Language version 2), a prominent protocol used for exchanging authentication and authorization data between identity providers and service providers.

**(a) What is SAMLv2?**

SAMLv2 is an XML-based open standard for secure exchange of authentication and authorization data. It enables Single Sign-On (SSO), allowing users to authenticate once and gain access to multiple applications without re-entering credentials. In the context of Azure AD, SAMLv2 facilitates secure communication between Azure AD (the identity provider) and various services (service providers) users want to access.

**(b) Implications of This Update**

*   **Enhanced Authentication:** Users can now authenticate through Azure AD when accessing a network via a captive portal. This means that organizations leveraging Azure AD for identity management can extend its use to captive portals, ensuring a consistent and secure authentication process.
    
*   **Single Sign-On (SSO):** With SAMLv2, users benefit from SSO capabilities. They log in once with their Azure AD credentials and gain seamless access to multiple services and applications without the need to re-authenticate, improving user experience and productivity.
    
*   **Increased Security:** SAMLv2 enhances security by enabling strong authentication and reducing password fatigue. It ensures that authentication tokens are securely transmitted and managed, protecting user credentials from potential attacks.
    

**(c) Practical Applications**

Organizations can now implement SAMLv2-based captive portals, allowing users to connect to networks using their Azure AD credentials. This integration streamlines access management and bolsters security, making it especially beneficial for enterprises with a high reliance on Azure AD for identity services.

In summary, the support for SAMLv2 in Azure-AD captive portals facilitates a more secure, efficient, and user-friendly authentication process, aligning with modern enterprise needs for robust identity and access management.

1.  **Support HTTPS-Only for local device page**
    

To address security concerns, we have introduced an HTTPS-only switch that allows users to control access to the Local Service Page (LSP). This feature is essential for enhancing the security of local device management by ensuring that all communications are encrypted.

**(a) Importance of HTTPS for Security**

HTTPS (Hypertext Transfer Protocol Secure) is an extension of HTTP and is widely used to secure data transmission over the internet. When enabled, HTTPS ensures that all data exchanged between the user's browser and the local device page is encrypted. This encryption is crucial for several reasons:

*   **Data Privacy:** HTTPS uses TLS (Transport Layer Security) to encrypt the data, making it unreadable to any third party that might intercept the communication. This protects sensitive information such as login credentials and configuration settings from being exposed.
    
*   **Data Integrity:** Encryption also ensures that the data transferred has not been altered during transmission. It prevents tampering and ensures that the information received by the user is exactly what the server sent.
    
*   **Authentication:** HTTPS verifies the identity of the local device page, ensuring that users are connecting to the correct page and not a malicious site impersonating it. This helps prevent man-in-the-middle attacks where an attacker might intercept and alter communications between the user and the device.
    
*   **User Trust:** Users are more likely to trust and engage with local device pages that employ HTTPS, as indicated by the padlock icon in the browser's address bar. This visual assurance helps build confidence in the security of the connection.
    

**(b) Implementation and Control**

By introducing an HTTPS-only switch, we empower users to enforce this level of security. Users can easily enable this switch to ensure that all access to the Local Service Page is through HTTPS. This change mitigates risks associated with unencrypted HTTP connections, such as eavesdropping and data breaches.

In summary, the HTTPS-only feature significantly enhances the security of local device pages by ensuring encrypted, authentic, and tamper-proof communication, thereby protecting user data and fostering trust.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/release-note/access-point-firmware/ecw536#v1.7.74)

v1.7.74

*   Fix the issue that AP sometimes goes offline even when the network is functioning normally.

*   Add multi-language support for System Name in LSP--You can modify the name of your AP from the cloud page where multiple languages are supported. Any changes made will synchronize to the LSP page “Device Overview” -> “System Name” field

Enjoy an updated interface that not only looks stylish but also aligns with contemporary design standards, providing a more visually pleasing and user-friendly experience.
    
*   Support shaping policies or block schemes on a per-application basis--Elevate network management with our SSID traffic throttling feature, now upgraded to customize bandwidth limits for specific applications such as YouTube, Apple iCloud, Facebook, Netflix, Apple App Store, and Line, etc. Facilitate enterprise clients to efficiently allocate limited bandwidth, ensuring optimal service delivery for a larger clientele.
    
*   If mDNS forwarding is enabled, BCMC suppression will not block mDNS packets.
    

1.  mDNS (Multicast DNS) Overview:
    
    mDNS, or Multicast DNS, is a protocol that allows devices on a local network to discover and connect to each other without the need for a centralized DNS (Domain Name System) server. It enables automatic assignment of domain names to devices, making it easier for users to access services on the network without manual configuration.
    
    In practical terms, mDNS simplifies the process of identifying and connecting to devices such as printers, smart home devices, and other networked services within a local environment. Instead of relying on traditional DNS, which typically involves a central server, mDNS uses multicast packets to resolve domain names to IP addresses directly on the local network.
    
2.  BCMC (Broadcast/Multicast Control) suppression Functionality:
    
    On the other hand, BCMC, or Broadcast/Multicast Control, is a feature designed to manage and control the impact of broadcast and multicast traffic on a network. Broadcasting and multicasting can lead to increased network congestion and reduced efficiency, especially in large-scale deployments.
    
    BCMC helps address these challenges by suppressing or controlling unnecessary broadcast and multicast traffic. By doing so, it ensures that the network operates more efficiently, reducing the risk of bandwidth saturation and enhancing overall performance.
    
3.  Interplay between mDNS and BCMC:
    
    In certain network scenarios, there may be a potential conflict between mDNS and BCMC functionalities. By allowing mDNS packets to pass through when mDNS forwarding is enabled, the network ensures that devices can continue to discover and communicate with each other seamlessly using the mDNS protocol. This synergy between mDNS and BCMC functionality aims to strike a balance between efficient network management and the need for smooth, decentralized device discovery and connectivity in local environments.
    

*   Client List supports more OS types - Meta VR devices, Honeywell IoT device…etc--Clients List feature now includes expanded compatibility with various operating systems such as Meta VR devices, Honeywell IoT devices, and more. To ensure ongoing accuracy and relevance, we regularly update our fingerprint identification system. This proactive approach allows us to seamlessly integrate newly released devices into the Cloud Clients List page, ensuring that you have precise and up-to-date information about connected clients.
    
*   SSID on LAN : support AD and LDAP captive portal authentication.
    
*   Disable 6GHz radio if selected Wi-Fi encryption is not supported on the 6GHz band.
    
*   Support 6GHz all-channel-utilization scan in diag tool.
    

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/release-note/access-point-firmware/ecw536#v1.7.60)

v1.7.60

### 

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/release-note/access-point-firmware/ecw526#appendix-for-v1.x.81)

**Appendix for v1.x.81**

1.  **Add support for SAMLv2 in Captive portal with Azure-AD**
    

A captive portal is a web page that users must interact with to gain network access, often seen in public Wi-Fi networks. This update introduces support for SAMLv2 (Security Assertion Markup Language version 2), a prominent protocol used for exchanging authentication and authorization data between identity providers and service providers.

**(a) What is SAMLv2?**

SAMLv2 is an XML-based open standard for secure exchange of authentication and authorization data. It enables Single Sign-On (SSO), allowing users to authenticate once and gain access to multiple applications without re-entering credentials. In the context of Azure AD, SAMLv2 facilitates secure communication between Azure AD (the identity provider) and various services (service providers) users want to access.

**(b) Implications of This Update**

*   **Enhanced Authentication:** Users can now authenticate through Azure AD when accessing a network via a captive portal. This means that organizations leveraging Azure AD for identity management can extend its use to captive portals, ensuring a consistent and secure authentication process.
    
*   **Single Sign-On (SSO):** With SAMLv2, users benefit from SSO capabilities. They log in once with their Azure AD credentials and gain seamless access to multiple services and applications without the need to re-authenticate, improving user experience and productivity.
    
*   **Increased Security:** SAMLv2 enhances security by enabling strong authentication and reducing password fatigue. It ensures that authentication tokens are securely transmitted and managed, protecting user credentials from potential attacks.
    

**(c) Practical Applications**

Organizations can now implement SAMLv2-based captive portals, allowing users to connect to networks using their Azure AD credentials. This integration streamlines access management and bolsters security, making it especially beneficial for enterprises with a high reliance on Azure AD for identity services.

In summary, the support for SAMLv2 in Azure-AD captive portals facilitates a more secure, efficient, and user-friendly authentication process, aligning with modern enterprise needs for robust identity and access management.

1.  **Support HTTPS-Only for local device page**
    

To address security concerns, we have introduced an HTTPS-only switch that allows users to control access to the Local Service Page (LSP). This feature is essential for enhancing the security of local device management by ensuring that all communications are encrypted.

**(a) Importance of HTTPS for Security**

HTTPS (Hypertext Transfer Protocol Secure) is an extension of HTTP and is widely used to secure data transmission over the internet. When enabled, HTTPS ensures that all data exchanged between the user's browser and the local device page is encrypted. This encryption is crucial for several reasons:

*   **Data Privacy:** HTTPS uses TLS (Transport Layer Security) to encrypt the data, making it unreadable to any third party that might intercept the communication. This protects sensitive information such as login credentials and configuration settings from being exposed.
    
*   **Data Integrity:** Encryption also ensures that the data transferred has not been altered during transmission. It prevents tampering and ensures that the information received by the user is exactly what the server sent.
    
*   **Authentication:** HTTPS verifies the identity of the local device page, ensuring that users are connecting to the correct page and not a malicious site impersonating it. This helps prevent man-in-the-middle attacks where an attacker might intercept and alter communications between the user and the device.
    
*   **User Trust:** Users are more likely to trust and engage with local device pages that employ HTTPS, as indicated by the padlock icon in the browser's address bar. This visual assurance helps build confidence in the security of the connection.
    

**(b) Implementation and Control**

By introducing an HTTPS-only switch, we empower users to enforce this level of security. Users can easily enable this switch to ensure that all access to the Local Service Page is through HTTPS. This change mitigates risks associated with unencrypted HTTP connections, such as eavesdropping and data breaches.

In summary, the HTTPS-only feature significantly enhances the security of local device pages by ensuring encrypted, authentic, and tamper-proof communication, thereby protecting user data and fostering trust.

[](https://docs.engenius.ai/release-note/access-point-firmware/ecw526#v1.8.75)
